```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-agent/src/index.ts</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: import { WebSocket } from "ws";
2: import { spawn, ChildProcess } from "child_process";
3: import { watch } from "fs";
4: import { join, relative } from "path";
5: 
6: interface AgentConfig {
7:   token: string;
8:   platform: string;
9:   workDir: string;
10: }
11: 
12: interface FileChange {
13:   path: string;
14:   isNew?: boolean;
15:   deleted?: boolean;
16: }
17: 
18: class MimoAgent {
19:   private ws: WebSocket | null = null;
20:   private config: AgentConfig;
21:   private acpProcess: ChildProcess | null = null;
22:   private fileWatcher: ReturnType<typeof watch> | null = null;
23:   private pendingChanges: FileChange[] = [];
24:   private changeTimeout: NodeJS.Timeout | null = null;
25:   private reconnectAttempts = 0;
26:   private maxReconnectAttempts = 5;
27:   private reconnectDelay = 1000;
28: 
29:   constructor() {
30:     this.config = this.parseArgs();
31:   }
32: 
33:   private parseArgs(): AgentConfig {
34:     const args = process.argv.slice(2);
35:     const config: Partial<AgentConfig> = {};
36: 
37:     for (let i = 0; i < args.length; i++) {
38:       const arg = args[i];
39:       if (arg === "--token" && i + 1 < args.length) {
40:         config.token = args[++i];
41:       } else if (arg === "--platform" && i + 1 < args.length) {
42:         config.platform = args[++i];
43:       } else if (arg === "--workdir" && i + 1 < args.length) {
44:         config.workDir = args[++i];
45:       }
46:     }
47: 
48:     if (!config.token) {
49:       throw new Error("Missing required argument: --token");
50:     }
51:     if (!config.platform) {
52:       throw new Error("Missing required argument: --platform");
53:     }
54: 
55:     // Default workDir to current directory if not specified
56:     if (!config.workDir) {
57:       config.workDir = process.cwd();
58:     }
59: 
60:     return config as AgentConfig;
61:   }
62: 
63:   async start(): Promise<void> {
64:     console.log("[mimo-agent] Starting...");
65:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Platform: ${this.config.platform}`);
66:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] WorkDir: ${this.config.workDir}`);
67: 
68:     // Start file watcher
69:     this.startFileWatcher();
70: 
71:     // Connect to platform
72:     await this.connect();
73: 
74:     // Handle graceful shutdown
75:     this.setupShutdownHandlers();
76:   }
77: 
78:   private async connect(): Promise<void> {
79:     const wsUrl = `${this.config.platform}?token=${this.config.token}`;
80:     
81:     return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
82:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Connecting to ${this.config.platform}...`);
83:       
84:       this.ws = new WebSocket(wsUrl);
85: 
86:       this.ws.on("open", () => {
87:         console.log("[mimo-agent] Connected to platform");
88:         this.reconnectAttempts = 0;
89:         
90:         // Send agent_ready message
91:         this.send({
92:           type: "agent_ready",
93:           timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
94:         });
95: 
96:         // Send any pending changes
97:         this.flushPendingChanges();
98:         
99:         resolve();
100:       });
101: 
102:       this.ws.on("message", (data: Buffer) => {
103:         try {
104:           const message = JSON.parse(data.toString());
105:           this.handleMessage(message);
106:         } catch (error) {
107:           console.error("[mimo-agent] Failed to parse message:", error);
108:         }
109:       });
110: 
111:       this.ws.on("close", (code: number, reason: Buffer) => {
112:         console.log(`[mimo-agent] Disconnected (code: ${code})`);
113:         this.handleDisconnect();
114:       });
115: 
116:       this.ws.on("error", (error: Error) => {
117:         console.error("[mimo-agent] WebSocket error:", error.message);
118:         reject(error);
119:       });
120: 
121:       // Connection timeout
122:       setTimeout(() => {
123:         if (this.ws?.readyState !== WebSocket.OPEN) {
124:           reject(new Error("Connection timeout"));
125:         }
126:       }, 10000);
127:     });
128:   }
129: 
130:   private handleMessage(message: any): void {
131:     switch (message.type) {
132:       case "ping":
133:         this.send({ type: "pong" });
134:         break;
135: 
136:       case "acp_request":
137:         this.handleAcpRequest(message);
138:         break;
139: 
140:       case "cancel_request":
141:         this.handleCancelRequest();
142:         break;
143: 
144:       case "file_sync_request":
145:         this.handleFileSyncRequest(message);
146:         break;
147: 
148:       default:
149:         console.log("[mimo-agent] Unknown message type:", message.type);
150:     }
151:   }
152: 
153:   private handleAcpRequest(message: any): void {
154:     if (this.acpProcess) {
155:       console.log("[mimo-agent] ACP process already running, terminating...");
156:       this.acpProcess.kill();
157:     }
158: 
159:     console.log("[mimo-agent] Starting ACP process...");
160:     
161:     // Spawn ACP agent (this would be the actual ACP SDK agent)
162:     // For now, we'll simulate with a basic command
163:     const acpCommand = message.command || "echo";
164:     const acpArgs = message.args || ["Simulated ACP response"];
165: 
166:     this.acpProcess = spawn(acpCommand, acpArgs, {
167:       cwd: this.config.workDir,
168:       stdio: ["pipe", "pipe", "pipe"],
169:     });
170: 
171:     // Proxy stdout to platform
172:     this.acpProcess.stdout?.on("data", (data: Buffer) => {
173:       this.send({
174:         type: "acp_response",
175:         content: data.toString(),
176:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
177:       });
178:     });
179: 
180:     // Handle stderr
181:     this.acpProcess.stderr?.on("data", (data: Buffer) => {
182:       console.error("[mimo-agent] ACP stderr:", data.toString());
183:     });
184: 
185:     // Handle process exit
186:     this.acpProcess.on("close", (code: number | null) => {
187:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] ACP process exited with code ${code}`);
188:       this.acpProcess = null;
189:     });
190:   }
191: 
192:   private handleCancelRequest(): void {
193:     if (this.acpProcess) {
194:       console.log("[mimo-agent] Cancelling ACP request...");
195:       this.acpProcess.kill("SIGTERM");
196:       this.acpProcess = null;
197:       
198:       this.send({
199:         type: "acp_cancelled",
200:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
201:       });
202:     } else {
203:       console.log("[mimo-agent] No active ACP request to cancel");
204:     }
205:   }
206: 
207:   private handleFileSyncRequest(message: any): void {
208:     // Respond with current file state if needed
209:     console.log("[mimo-agent] File sync request received");
210:   }
211: 
212:   private handleDisconnect(): void {
213:     if (this.reconnectAttempts < this.maxReconnectAttempts) {
214:       this.reconnectAttempts++;
215:       const delay = this.reconnectDelay * Math.pow(2, this.reconnectAttempts - 1);
216:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Reconnecting in ${delay}ms (attempt ${this.reconnectAttempts})...`);
217:       
218:       setTimeout(() => {
219:         this.connect().catch((error) => {
220:           console.error("[mimo-agent] Reconnect failed:", error.message);
221:         });
222:       }, delay);
223:     } else {
224:       console.error("[mimo-agent] Max reconnect attempts reached, exiting");
225:       process.exit(1);
226:     }
227:   }
228: 
229:   private startFileWatcher(): void {
230:     console.log("[mimo-agent] Starting file watcher...");
231: 
232:     this.fileWatcher = watch(
233:       this.config.workDir,
234:       { recursive: true },
235:       (eventType: string, filename: string | null) => {
236:         if (!filename) return;
237:         
238:         // Skip hidden files and common ignore patterns
239:         if (filename.startsWith(".") || filename.includes("/.") || 
240:             filename.includes("node_modules") || filename.includes("__pycache__") ||
241:             filename.endsWith(".tmp") || filename.endsWith("~")) {
242:           return;
243:         }
244: 
245:         const filePath = filename;
246:         const change: FileChange = {
247:           path: filePath,
248:           isNew: eventType === "rename",
249:           deleted: false, // We'll detect deletions differently
250:         };
251: 
252:         // Buffer changes to batch them
253:         this.pendingChanges.push(change);
254:         
255:         // Debounce changes
256:         if (this.changeTimeout) {
257:           clearTimeout(this.changeTimeout);
258:         }
259:         
260:         this.changeTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
261:           this.flushPendingChanges();
262:         }, 500);
263:       }
264:     );
265:   }
266: 
267:   private flushPendingChanges(): void {
268:     if (this.pendingChanges.length === 0) return;
269: 
270:     const changes = [...this.pendingChanges];
271:     this.pendingChanges = [];
272: 
273:     // Deduplicate changes
274:     const uniqueChanges = new Map<string, FileChange>();
275:     for (const change of changes) {
276:       uniqueChanges.set(change.path, change);
277:     }
278: 
279:     this.send({
280:       type: "file_changed",
281:       files: Array.from(uniqueChanges.values()),
282:       timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
283:     });
284:   }
285: 
286:   private send(message: any): void {
287:     if (this.ws?.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
288:       this.ws.send(JSON.stringify(message));
289:     } else {
290:       // Buffer message if not connected
291:       console.log("[mimo-agent] WebSocket not connected, message buffered");
292:     }
293:   }
294: 
295:   private setupShutdownHandlers(): void {
296:     const shutdown = () => {
297:       console.log("[mimo-agent] Shutting down gracefully...");
298:       
299:       // Kill ACP process if running
300:       if (this.acpProcess) {
301:         this.acpProcess.kill("SIGTERM");
302:       }
303: 
304:       // Close file watcher
305:       if (this.fileWatcher) {
306:         this.fileWatcher.close();
307:       }
308: 
309:       // Close WebSocket
310:       if (this.ws) {
311:         this.ws.close();
312:       }
313: 
314:       process.exit(0);
315:     };
316: 
317:     process.on("SIGTERM", shutdown);
318:     process.on("SIGINT", shutdown);
319:     process.on("SIGUSR2", shutdown); // For Windows
320: 
321:     // Handle uncaught errors
322:     process.on("uncaughtException", (error) => {
323:       console.error("[mimo-agent] Uncaught exception:", error);
324:       shutdown();
325:     });
326: 
327:     process.on("unhandledRejection", (reason) => {
328:       console.error("[mimo-agent] Unhandled rejection:", reason);
329:     });
330:   }
331: }
332: 
333: // Start the agent
334: const agent = new MimoAgent();
335: agent.start().catch((error) => {
336:   console.error("[mimo-agent] Failed to start:", error.message);
337:   process.exit(1);
338: });

(End of file - total 338 lines)
</content>
```

```
84: const server = Bun.serve({

100:             break;
101:           default:
102:             console.log("Unknown connection type");
103:         }
104:       } catch (error) {
105:         console.error("WebSocket message error:", error);
106:       }
107:     },
108:     async open(ws) {
109:       const url = new URL(ws.data.url);
110:       const type = url.pathname.split('/')[2]; // /ws/chat or /ws/agent
111:       
112:       if (type === 'chat') {
113:         // Chat connection
114:         const sessionId = url.pathname.split('/')[3];
115:         ws.data.connectionType = 'chat';
116:         ws.data.sessionId = sessionId;
117:         
118:         // Add to session subscribers
119:         if (!chatSessions.has(sessionId)) {
120:           chatSessions.set(sessionId, new Set());
121:         }
122:         chatSessions.get(sessionId).add(ws);
123:         
124:         // Send chat history
125:         const history = await chatService.loadHistory(sessionId);
126:         ws.send(JSON.stringify({
127:           type: 'history',
128:           messages: history,
129:         }));
130:         
131:         console.log(`Chat client connected to session ${sessionId}`);
132:       } else {
133:         // Agent connection
134:         const token = url.searchParams.get("token");
135:         
136:         if (!token) {
137:           ws.close(1008, "Missing token");
138:           return;
139:         }
140: 
141:         const payload = await agentService.verifyAgentToken(token);
142:         if (!payload) {
143:           ws.close(1008, "Invalid token");
144:           return;
145:         }
146: 
147:         ws.data.connectionType = 'agent';
148:         ws.data.agentId = payload.agentId;
149:         
150:         await agentService.handleAgentConnect(payload.agentId, ws);
151:         console.log(`Agent ${payload.agentId} connected`);
152:       }
153:     },
154:     async close(ws) {
155:       const connectionType = ws.data?.connectionType;
156:       
157:       if (connectionType === 'chat') {
158:         // Remove from session subscribers
159:         const sessionId = ws.data.sessionId;
160:         if (chatSessions.has(sessionId)) {
161:           chatSessions.get(sessionId).delete(ws);
162:           if (chatSessions.get(sessionId).size === 0) {
163:             chatSessions.delete(sessionId);
164:           }
165:         }
166:         console.log(`Chat client disconnected from session ${sessionId}`);
167:       } else if (connectionType === 'agent') {
168:         const agentId = ws.data.agentId;
169:         if (agentId) {
170:           await agentService.handleAgentDisconnect(agentId);
171:           console.log(`Agent ${agentId} disconnected`);
172:         }
173:       }
174:     },
175:   },
176: });
177: 
178: // Handle agent messages
179: async function handleAgentMessage(ws, data) {
180:   switch (data.type) {
181:     case "ping":
182:       ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: "pong" }));
183:       break;
184:     case "agent_ready":
185:       console.log("Agent ready:", data.agentId);
186:       break;
187:     case "acp_response":
188:       // Handle ACP response and broadcast to chat
189:       // Agent must specify which session this is for
190:       const sessionId = data.sessionId;
191:       if (!sessionId) {
192:         console.log("No sessionId in acp_response");
193:         return;
194:       }
195:       
196:       // Broadcast to all chat clients in session
197:       const subscribers = chatSessions.get(sessionId);
198:       if (subscribers) {
199:         subscribers.forEach(client => {
200:           if (client.readyState === 1) { // WebSocket.OPEN
201:             client.send(JSON.stringify({
202:               type: 'message',
203:               role: 'assistant',
204:               content: data.content,
205:               timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
206:             }));
207:           }
208:         });
209:       }
210:       
211:       // Save to history
212:       await chatService.saveMessage(sessionId, {
213:         role: 'assistant',
214:         content: data.content,
215:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
216:       });
217:       break;
218:     case "file_changed":
219:       console.log("File changed:", data.files);
220:       
221:       const fileSessionId = data.sessionId;
222:       if (!fileSessionId) {
223:         console.log("No sessionId in file_changed");
224:         return;
225:       }
226:       
227:       const changes = data.files.map((file) => ({
228:         path: file.path,
229:         isNew: file.isNew,
230:         deleted: file.deleted,
231:       }));
232:       
233:       await fileSyncService.initializeSession(fileSessionId, "", "");
234:       await fileSyncService.handleFileChanges(fileSessionId, changes);
235:       break;
236:     default:
237:       console.log("Unknown agent message type:", data.type);
238:   }
239: }
240: 
241: // Handle chat messages
242: async function handleChatMessage(ws, data) {
243:   const sessionId = ws.data.sessionId;
244:   
245:   switch (data.type) {
246:     case "send_message":
247:       // Save user message
248:       await chatService.saveMessage(sessionId, {
249:         role: 'user',
250:         content: data.content,
251:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
252:       });
253:       
254:       // Broadcast to all clients in session
255:       const subscribers = chatSessions.get(sessionId);
256:       if (subscribers) {
257:         subscribers.forEach(client => {
258:           if (client.readyState === 1) {
259:             client.send(JSON.stringify({
260:               type: 'message',
261:               role: 'user',
262:               content: data.content,
263:               timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
264:             }));
265:           }
266:         });
267:       }
268:       
269:       // Get session to find assigned agent
270:       const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
271:       if (session?.assignedAgentId) {
272:         // Forward to agent if connected
273:         const ws = agentService.getAgentConnection(session.assignedAgentId);
274:         if (ws && ws.readyState === 1) {
275:           ws.send(JSON.stringify({
276:             type: 'user_message',
277:             sessionId: sessionId,
278:             content: data.content,
279:           }));
280:         }
281:       }
282:       break;
283:       
284:     case "request_replay":
285:       const history = await chatService.loadHistory(sessionId);
286:       ws.send(JSON.stringify({
287:         type: 'history',
288:         messages: history,
289:       }));
290:       break;
291:       
292:     default:
293:       console.log("Unknown chat message type:", data.type);
294:   }
295: }
296: 
297: // Server is ready
298: console.log(`Server running at http://localhost:${server.port}`);

(End of file - total 298 lines)
</content>
```

```
<content>1: import { Agent, AgentRepository, AgentStatus, agentRepository } from "./repository.js";
2: import { SignJWT, jwtVerify } from "jose";
3: 
4: const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || "your-secret-key-change-in-production";
5: const AGENT_SECRET = new TextEncoder().encode(JWT_SECRET);
6: 
7: export interface AgentTokenPayload {
8:   agentId: string;
9:   owner: string;
10: }
11: 
12: export interface CreateAgentInput {
13:   owner: string;
14: }
15: 
16: export class AgentService {
17:   private activeConnections: Map<string, WebSocket> = new Map();
18:   private currentAcpRequest: Map<string, AbortController> = new Map();
19: 
20:   constructor(
21:     private repository: AgentRepository = agentRepository
22:   ) {}
23: 
24:   async createAgent(input: CreateAgentInput): Promise<Agent> {
25:     const agent = await this.repository.create({
26:       owner: input.owner,
27:     });
28: 
29:     const token = await this.generateAgentToken(agent);
30:     await this.repository.update(agent.id, { token });
31:     
32:     return { ...agent, token };
33:   }
34: 
35:   async generateAgentToken(agent: Agent): Promise<string> {
36:     const token = await new SignJWT({
37:       agentId: agent.id,
38:       owner: agent.owner,
39:     })
40:       .setProtectedHeader({ alg: "HS256" })
41:       .setIssuedAt()
42:       .setExpirationTime("24h")
43:       .sign(AGENT_SECRET);
44: 
45:     return token;
46:   }
47: 
48:   async verifyAgentToken(token: string): Promise<AgentTokenPayload | null> {
49:     try {
50:       const { payload } = await jwtVerify(token, AGENT_SECRET);
51:       return {
52:         agentId: payload.agentId as string,
53:         owner: payload.owner as string,
54:       };
55:     } catch {
56:       return null;
57:     }
58:   }
59: 
60:   async handleAgentConnect(agentId: string, ws: WebSocket): Promise<void> {
61:     const agent = await this.repository.findById(agentId);
62:     if (!agent) {
63:       ws.close(1008, "Agent not found");
64:       return;
65:     }
66: 
67:     this.activeConnections.set(agentId, ws);
68:     await this.repository.updateStatus(agentId, "online");
69:     await this.repository.updateLastActivity(agentId);
70:   }
71: 
72:   async handleAgentDisconnect(agentId: string): Promise<void> {
73:     this.activeConnections.delete(agentId);
74:     await this.repository.updateStatus(agentId, "offline");
75:   }
76: 
77:   async cancelCurrentRequest(sessionId: string): Promise<boolean> {
78:     const sessionRepo = await import("../sessions/repository.js");
79:     const session = await sessionRepo.sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
80:     if (!session || !session.assignedAgentId) {
81:       return false;
82:     }
83: 
84:     const agent = await this.repository.findById(session.assignedAgentId);
85:     if (!agent || agent.status !== "online") {
86:       return false;
87:     }
88: 
89:     const controller = this.currentAcpRequest.get(session.assignedAgentId);
90:     if (controller) {
91:       controller.abort();
92:       this.currentAcpRequest.delete(session.assignedAgentId);
93:     }
94: 
95:     const ws = this.activeConnections.get(session.assignedAgentId);
96:     if (ws) {
97:       ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: "cancel_request" }));
98:     }
99: 
100:     return true;
101:   }
102: 
103:   async deleteAgent(agentId: string): Promise<boolean> {
104:     const agent = await this.repository.findById(agentId);
105:     if (!agent) return false;
106: 
107:     if (this.activeConnections.has(agentId)) {
108:       const ws = this.activeConnections.get(agentId);
109:       ws?.close(1000, "Agent deleted");
110:       this.activeConnections.delete(agentId);
111:     }
112: 
113:     this.currentAcpRequest.delete(agentId);
114:     await this.repository.delete(agentId);
115:     
116:     return true;
117:   }
118: 
119:   async getAgentStatus(agentId: string): Promise<Agent | null> {
120:     return this.repository.findById(agentId);
121:   }
122: 
123:   async listAgentsByOwner(owner: string): Promise<Agent[]> {
124:     return this.repository.findByOwner(owner);
125:   }
126: 
127:   async listAgentsByStatus(status: AgentStatus): Promise<Agent[]> {
128:     return this.repository.findByStatus(status);
129:   }
130: 
131:   isAgentOnline(agentId: string): boolean {
132:     return this.activeConnections.has(agentId);
133:   }
134: 
135:   getAgentConnection(agentId: string): WebSocket | undefined {
136:     return this.activeConnections.get(agentId);
137:   }
138: 
139:   startAcpRequest(agentId: string): AbortController {
140:     const controller = new AbortController();
141:     this.currentAcpRequest.set(agentId, controller);
142:     return controller;
143:   }
144: 
145:   endAcpRequest(agentId: string): void {
146:     this.currentAcpRequest.delete(agentId);
147:   }
148: 
149:   async sendToAgent(agentId: string, message: unknown): Promise<boolean> {
150:     const ws = this.activeConnections.get(agentId);
151:     if (!ws) return false;
152: 
153:     try {
154:       ws.send(JSON.stringify(message));
155:       return true;
156:     } catch {
157:       return false;
158:     }
159:   }
160: }
```

```typescript
}
```

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 00:48:53)

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 00:49:10)

The issue is the Bun.serve configuration. The `websocket` object defines handlers for `message`, `open`, `close`, but the `fetch` function is `app.fetch`. 

For Bun WebSocket upgrades, the `fetch` function needs to return a server upgrade response when a WebSocket request comes in. But here it's using `app.fetch` which doesn't handle upgrades.

The typical pattern in Bun is:
```typescript
const server = Bun.serve({
  fetch(req, server) {
    const url = new URL(req.url);
    if (url.pathname === "/ws/agent" && req.headers.get("upgrade") === "websocket") {
      server.upgrade(req, { data: { ... } });
      return;
    }
    return app.fetch(req);
  },
  websocket: { ... }
});
```

But the current code just uses `app.fetch` which doesn't handle WebSocket upgrades - it just returns 404.
## Agent (2026-04-04 00:49:12)

Found the issue. The Bun server configuration is missing WebSocket upgrade handling. The `fetch: app.fetch` doesn't handle WebSocket upgrade requests - it needs a custom handler. Here's the fix:

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/index.tsx

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 00:49:15
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/index.tsx
oldString: const server = Bun.serve({
  fetch: app.fetch,
  port: PORT,
  websocket: {
newString: const server = Bun.serve({
  async fetch(req: Request, server: any) {
    const url = new URL(req.url);
    
    // Handle WebSocket upgrade requests
    if (req.headers.get("upgrade") === "websocket") {
      const type = url.pathname.split('/')[2]; // /ws/agent or /ws/chat
      
      if (type === 'agent') {
        const token = url.searchParams.get("token");
        if (!token) {
          return new Response("Missing token", { status: 400 });
        }
        
        const payload = await agentService.verifyAgentToken(token);
        if (!payload) {
          return new Response("Invalid token", { status: 401 });
        }
        
        const upgraded = server.upgrade(req, {
          data: {
            connectionType: 'agent',
            agentId: payload.agentId,
            url: req.url
          }
        });
        
        if (!upgraded) {
          return new Response("WebSocket upgrade failed", { status: 500 });
        }
        return undefined;
      }
      
      if (type === 'chat') {
        const sessionId = url.pathname.split('/')[3];
        if (!sessionId) {
          return new Response("Missing sessionId", { status: 400 });
        }
        
        const upgraded = server.upgrade(req, {
          data: {
            connectionType: 'chat',
            sessionId,
            url: req.url
          }
        });
        
        if (!upgraded) {
          return new Response("WebSocket upgrade failed", { status: 500 });
        }
        return undefined;
      }
      
      return new Response("Unknown WebSocket endpoint", { status: 404 });
    }
    
    return app.fetch(req);
  },
  port: PORT,
  websocket: {

```

45: function renderFileTree(changes: FileChange[]) {
46:   const fileTree: Map<string, { name: string; status: FileChange["status"] }[]> = new Map();
47:   
48:   for (const change of changes) {
49:     const parts = change.path.split("/");
50:     const fileName = parts.pop() || "";
51:     const dir = parts.length > 0 ? parts.join("/") : "(root)";
52:     
53:     if (!fileTree.has(dir)) {
54:       fileTree.set(dir, []);
55:     }
56:     fileTree.get(dir)!.push({ name: fileName, status: change.status });
57:   }
58:   
59:   const sortedDirs = Array.from(fileTree.entries()).sort((a, b) => a[0].localeCompare(b[0]));

64:         <div key={dir} class="file-tree-dir">

66:           <div class="file-tree-files">
67:             {files.map((file) => (
68:               <div key={file.name} class="file-tree-file">
69:                 <span class={`file-indicator file-indicator-${file.status}`}>
70:                   {file.status === "modified" && "[M]"}
71:                   {file.status === "new" && "[?]"}
72:                   {file.status === "deleted" && "[D]"}
73:                   {file.status === "conflict" && "[!]"}
74:                   {file.status === "clean" && "   "}
75:                 </span>
76:                 <span class={`file-name file-name-${file.status}`}>{file.name}</span>
77:               </div>
78:             ))}
79:           </div>
80:         </div>
81:       ))}
82:     </div>
83:   );
84: }
85: 
86: function getStatusIcon(status: FileChange["status"]): string {
87:   switch (status) {
88:     case "modified": return "M";
89:     case "new": return "?";
90:     case "deleted": return "D";
91:     case "conflict": return "!";
92:     default: return " ";
93:   }
94: }
95:
```

```
<content>1: import { join } from "path";
2: import { existsSync, mkdirSync, writeFileSync, readFileSync, readdirSync, rmdirSync, unlinkSync } from "fs";
3: import { getPaths } from "../config/paths.js";
4: import { dump, load } from "js-yaml";
5: import crypto from "crypto";
6: 
7: export interface Session {
8:   id: string;
9:   name: string;
10:   projectId: string;
11:   owner: string;
12:   worktreePath: string;
13:   assignedAgentId?: string;
14:   status: "active" | "paused" | "closed";
15:   createdAt: Date;
16:   updatedAt: Date;
17: }
18: 
19: export interface SessionData {
20:   id: string;
21:   name: string;
22:   projectId: string;
23:   owner: string;
24:   worktreePath: string;
25:   assignedAgentId?: string;
26:   status: "active" | "paused" | "closed";
27:   createdAt: string;
28:   updatedAt: string;
29: }
30: 
31: export interface CreateSessionInput {
32:   name: string;
33:   projectId: string;
34:   owner: string;
35:   worktreePath: string;
36:   assignedAgentId?: string;
37: }
38: 
39: export class SessionRepository {
40:   private getSessionPath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
41:     return join(getPaths().projects, projectId, "sessions", sessionId);
42:   }
43: 
44:   private getSessionFilePath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
45:     return join(this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId), "session.yaml");
46:   }
47: 
48:   private generateId(): string {
49:     return crypto.randomUUID();
50:   }
51: 
52:   private getWorktreePath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
53:     return join(getPaths().projects, projectId, "worktrees", sessionId);
54:   }
55: 
56:   async create(input: CreateSessionInput): Promise<Session> {
57:     const id = this.generateId();
58:     const sessionPath = this.getSessionPath(input.projectId, id);
59:     const worktreePath = this.getWorktreePath(input.projectId, id);
60:     
61:     // Create session directory
62:     if (!existsSync(sessionPath)) {
63:       mkdirSync(sessionPath, { recursive: true });
64:     }
65: 
66:     // Create worktree directory
67:     if (!existsSync(worktreePath)) {
68:       mkdirSync(worktreePath, { recursive: true });
69:     }
70: 
71:     const now = new Date().toISOString();
72:     const sessionData: SessionData = {
73:       id,
74:       name: input.name,
75:       projectId: input.projectId,
76:       owner: input.owner,
77:       worktreePath,
78:       assignedAgentId: input.assignedAgentId,
79:       status: "active",
80:       createdAt: now,
81:       updatedAt: now,
82:     };
83: 
84:     writeFileSync(
85:       this.getSessionFilePath(input.projectId, id),
86:       dump(sessionData),
87:       "utf-8"
88:     );
89: 
90:     return {
91:       ...sessionData,
92:       createdAt: new Date(sessionData.createdAt),
93:       updatedAt: new Date(sessionData.updatedAt),
94:     };
95:   }
96: 
97:   async findById(sessionId: string): Promise<Session | null> {
98:     // Search across all projects for the session
99:     const Paths = getPaths();
100:     if (!existsSync(Paths.projects)) {
101:       return null;
102:     }
103: 
104:     const projectEntries = readdirSync(Paths.projects, { withFileTypes: true });
105:     
106:     for (const projectEntry of projectEntries) {
107:       if (projectEntry.isDirectory()) {
108:         const sessionsDir = join(Paths.projects, projectEntry.name, "sessions");
109:         if (existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
110:           const sessionFile = join(sessionsDir, sessionId, "session.yaml");
111:           if (existsSync(sessionFile)) {
112:             const content = readFileSync(sessionFile, "utf-8");
113:             const data = load(content) as SessionData;
114:             return {
115:               ...data,
116:               createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
117:               updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
118:             };
119:           }
120:         }
121:       }
122:     }
123: 
124:     return null;
125:   }
126: 
127:   async findByProjectAndId(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<Session | null> {
128:     const filePath = this.getSessionFilePath(projectId, sessionId);
129:     if (!existsSync(filePath)) {
130:       return null;
131:     }
132: 
133:     const content = readFileSync(filePath, "utf-8");
134:     const data = load(content) as SessionData;
135:     
136:     return {
137:       ...data,
138:       createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
139:       updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
140:     };
141:   }
142: 
143:   async listByProject(projectId: string): Promise<Session[]> {
144:     const sessionsDir = join(getPaths().projects, projectId, "sessions");
145:     if (!existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
146:       return [];
147:     }
148: 
149:     const entries = readdirSync(sessionsDir, { withFileTypes: true });
150:     const sessions: Session[] = [];
151: 
152:     for (const entry of entries) {
153:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
154:         const sessionFile = join(sessionsDir, entry.name, "session.yaml");
155:         if (existsSync(sessionFile)) {
156:           const content = readFileSync(sessionFile, "utf-8");
157:           const data = load(content) as SessionData;
158:           sessions.push({
159:             ...data,
160:             createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
161:             updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
162:           });
163:         }
164:       }
165:     }
166: 
167:     return sessions.sort((a, b) => b.createdAt.getTime() - a.createdAt.getTime());
168:   }
169: 
170:   async findByAssignedAgentId(agentId: string): Promise<Session[]> {
171:     const Paths = getPaths();
172:     if (!existsSync(Paths.projects)) {
173:       return [];
174:     }
175: 
176:     const projectEntries = readdirSync(Paths.projects, { withFileTypes: true });
177:     const sessions: Session[] = [];
178: 
179:     for (const projectEntry of projectEntries) {
180:       if (projectEntry.isDirectory()) {
181:         const sessionsDir = join(Paths.projects, projectEntry.name, "sessions");
182:         if (existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
183:           const entries = readdirSync(sessionsDir, { withFileTypes: true });
184:           for (const entry of entries) {
185:             if (entry.isDirectory()) {
186:               const sessionFile = join(sessionsDir, entry.name, "session.yaml");
187:               if (existsSync(sessionFile)) {
188:                 const content = readFileSync(sessionFile, "utf-8");
189:                 const data = load(content) as SessionData;
190:                 if (data.assignedAgentId === agentId) {
191:                   sessions.push({
192:                     ...data,
193:                     createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
194:                     updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
195:                   });
196:                 }
197:               }
198:             }
199:           }
200:         }
201:       }
202:     }
203: 
204:     return sessions.sort((a, b) => b.createdAt.getTime() - a.createdAt.getTime());
205:   }
206: 
207:   async update(sessionId: string, updates: Partial<Omit<SessionData, "id" | "createdAt">>): Promise<Session | null> {
208:     const session = await this.findById(sessionId);
209:     if (!session) return null;
210: 
211:     const updatedData: SessionData = {
212:       ...session,
213:       ...updates,
214:       updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
215:     };
216: 
217:     const filePath = this.getSessionFilePath(session.projectId, sessionId);
218:     writeFileSync(filePath, dump(updatedData), "utf-8");
219: 
220:     return {
221:       ...updatedData,
222:       createdAt: new Date(updatedData.createdAt),
223:       updatedAt: new Date(updatedData.updatedAt),
224:     };
225:   }
226: 
227:   async delete(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
228:     const sessionPath = this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId);
229:     
230:     // Get session to find worktree path
231:     const session = await this.findByProjectAndId(projectId, sessionId);
232:     
233:     if (session && existsSync(session.worktreePath)) {
234:       // Delete worktree directory
235:       this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(session.worktreePath);
236:     }
237:     
238:     // Delete session directory
239:     if (existsSync(sessionPath)) {
240:       this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(sessionPath);
241:     }
242:   }
243: 
244:   private deleteDirectoryRecursive(dirPath: string): void {
245:     if (!existsSync(dirPath)) return;
246: 
247:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
248:     
249:     for (const entry of entries) {
250:       const entryPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
251:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
252:         this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(entryPath);
253:       } else {
254:         unlinkSync(entryPath);
255:       }
256:     }
257: 
258:     rmdirSync(dirPath);
259:   }
260: 
261:   async exists(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<boolean> {
262:     return existsSync(this.getSessionFilePath(projectId, sessionId));
263:   }
264: }
```

```
8: export class VCS {
9:   private async execCommand(
10:     command: string[],
11:     cwd?: string
12:   ): Promise<{ success: boolean; output: string; error: string }> {
13:     const proc = Bun.spawn(command, {
14:       cwd,
15:       stdout: "pipe",
16:       stderr: "pipe",
17:     });
18: 
19:     const exitCode = await proc.exited;
20:     const stdout = await new Response(proc.stdout).text();
21:     const stderr = await new Response(proc.stderr).text();
22: 
23:     return {
24:       success: exitCode === 0,
25:       output: stdout.trim(),
26:       error: stderr.trim(),
27:     };
28:   }
29: 
30:   async checkFossilAvailable(): Promise<boolean> {
31:     const result = await this.execCommand(["fossil", "version"]);
32:     return result.success;
33:   }
34: 
35:   async getFossilVersion(): Promise<string | null> {
36:     const result = await this.execCommand(["fossil", "version"]);
37:     if (result.success) {
38:       const match = result.output.match(/(\d+\.\d+)/);
39:       return match ? match[1] : null;
40:     }
41:     return null;
42:   }
43: 
44:   async createFossilRepo(repoPath: string): Promise<VCSResult> {
45:     const result = await this.execCommand(["fossil", "init", repoPath]);
46:     return {
47:       success: result.success,
48:       output: result.output,
49:       error: result.error || undefined,
50:     };

57:     );
58:     return {
59:       success: result.success,
60:       output: result.output,
61:       error: result.error || undefined,
62:     };

65:   async importGitToFossil(gitUrl: string, workDir: string): Promise<VCSResult> {
66:     try {
67:       new URL(gitUrl);
68:     } catch {
69:       return {
70:         success: false,
71:         error: "Invalid Git URL format",
72:       };
73:     }
74: 
75:     // Create fossil repo first
76:     const fossilPath = `${workDir}/.fossil`;
77:     const initResult = await this.createFossilRepo(fossilPath);
78:     if (!initResult.success) {
79:       return initResult;
80:     }
81: 
82:     // Import from git
83:     const result = await this.execCommand(
84:       ["fossil", "import", "--git", gitUrl, fossilPath],
85:       workDir
86:     );
87: 
88:     if (result.success) {
89:       // Open the fossil repo in the workdir
90:       const openResult = await this.openFossil(fossilPath, workDir);
91:       return openResult;
92:     }
93: 
94:     return {
95:       success: false,
96:       output: result.output,
97:       error: result.error || "Failed to import from Git",
98:     };
99:   }
100: 
101:   async cloneFossil(
102:     sourcePath: string,
103:     targetDir: string
104:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
105:     const { mkdirSync } = await import("fs");
106:     const { dirname } = await import("path");
107: 
108:     // Ensure target directory exists
109:     try {
110:       mkdirSync(targetDir, { recursive: true });
111:     } catch {
112:       // Directory might already exist
113:     }
114: 
115:     // Clone the fossil repo
116:     const result = await this.execCommand([
117:       "fossil",
118:       "clone",
119:       sourcePath,
120:       `${targetDir}/.fossil`,
121:     ]);
122: 
123:     if (result.success) {
124:       // Open the cloned repo
125:       const openResult = await this.openFossil(
126:         `${targetDir}/.fossil`,
127:         targetDir
128:       );
129:       return openResult;
130:     }
131: 
132:     return {
133:       success: false,
134:       output: result.output,
135:       error: result.error || "Failed to clone Fossil repository",
136:     };
137:   }

141:     direction: "pull" | "push"
142:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
143:     const command = direction === "pull" ? "pull" : "push";
144:     const result = await this.execCommand(["fossil", command], workDir);
145:
```

Now I'm getting a clearer picture. Let me trace through what happens:

1. When creating a session, `sessionRepository.create()` is called

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 00:54:59)

Now I see the picture. Let me trace through what happens when:

1. **Creating a project** - Stores metadata (project.yaml) but doesn't clone the repo
2. **Creating a session** - Creates session metadata + worktree directory + calls `vcs.setupSessionWorktree()`

But `setupSessionWorktree` tries to open a fossil repo at `${projectPath}/repo.fossil` which doesn't exist because:

1. When project is created, no fossil repo is initialized
2. No git clone happens
3. No conversion to fossil happens

The current flow:

```
Create Project → Store metadata in project.yaml → NO REPO CLONE
                           ↓
Create Session → Create worktrees/session-xyz/ directory
                           ↓
               vcs.setupSessionWorktree(projectId, sessionId, worktreePath)
                           ↓
               Opens repo.fossil from project dir → FAILS (doesn't exist)
```

What I think should happen:

```
Create Project → Store metadata in project.yaml
                           ↓
               Clone git repo OR copy fossil repo
                           ↓
               Create local fossil repo for tracking
                           ↓
Create Session → Create worktrees/session-xyz/
                           ↓
               Open fossil repo in worktree
```

Let me check if there's any initialization logic for the project repository.

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 00:55:04)

Let me understand the flow:

1. **Project Creation** (`projects/routes.tsx`):
   - Creates a project record with `repoUrl` and `repoType`
   - Does NOT clone any repository
   - Just stores metadata in `project.yaml`

2. **Session Creation** (`sessions/routes.tsx`):
   - Creates a session record in `sessions/<sessionId>/session.yaml`
   - Creates a worktree directory at `projects/<projectId>/worktrees/<sessionId>`
   - Calls `vcs.setupSessionWorktree()` which:
     - Looks for `repo.fossil` at `projects/<projectId>/repo.fossil`
     - Opens it in the worktree

**The Problems:**

1. **No project repository initialization**: When a project is created, there's no code to:
   - Clone the git repository
   - Or create/import into a fossil repository

2. **Session worktree expects a fossil repo**: `setupSessionWorktree` looks for `repo.fossil` but that file is never created during project creation.

3. **No proxy repository for mimo-agent**: There's no mechanism to create a "proxy" repository that the mimo-agent would clone and work with.

Let me check if there's any initialization code I missed:

## What's Missing

1. **When a project is created from a git URL**:
   - Should create `repo.fossil` in the project directory
   - Should import the git repository into fossil
   - Should open a working checkout

2. **When a session is created**:
   - Relies on `repo.fossil` already existing
   - Opens the fossil repository into the worktree
   - Currently fails silently because repo.fossil doesn't exist

Let me check if there's any code that should be doing this:

```
│       └── (empty dir)      ❌ No files tracked                                │
│                                                                               │
├──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                               │
│  mimo-agent (remote):                                                        │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐        │
│  │ What it needs:                                                   │        │
│  │   ├─ Clone the PROXY repository to /tmp/demo                     │        │
│  │   └─ Watch file changes and report to platform                  │        │
│  │                                                                  │        │
│  │ What's missing:                                                  │        │
│  │   ├─ No proxy repository exists!                                │        │
│  │   ├─ Agent has nowhere to clone FROM                            │        │

```

The architecture has two key missing pieces:

1. **Project creation should convert git → fossil**: When a user creates a project with a git URL, the system should:
   - Clone/import the git repo into a Fossil repo (`repo.fossil`)
   - Store this at `~/.mimo/projects/<id>/repo.fossil`

2. **Proxy repository for agent**: The mimo-agent needs:
   - A way to get the code to work with
   - The token includes `sessionId` and `projectId`, suggesting the agent should receive:
     - A clone URL (or the platform should serve one)
     - Or the worktree should be served somehow

Let me check if there's any design about this proxy repo concept, or if the agent is supposed to work differently.

````
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/README.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: # MIMO Platform
2: 
3: A minimal, Emacs-style web-based editor for AI-assisted development.
4: 
5: ## Overview
6: 
7: MIMO (Minimal IDE for Modern Operations) is a platform that enables AI-assisted development through a web-based interface with an Emacs-style workflow. It provides session-based development with worktrees, file synchronization, and integrated chat with AI agents.
8: 
9: ## Features
10: 
11: - **Public Landing Page**: View platform overview and public projects without authentication
12: - **Project Descriptions**: Add optional descriptions to projects for better discoverability
13: - **Emacs-Style Interface**: Three-buffer layout with customizable keybindings
14: - **Session-Based Development**: Work with isolated worktrees for each development session
15: - **File Synchronization**: Automatic sync between agent worktree and original repository
16: - **Integrated Chat**: Real-time chat with AI agents via WebSocket
17: - **VCS Integration**: Fossil as intermediary for both Git and Fossil repositories
18: - **Agent Lifecycle**: Spawn and manage AI agents with JWT authentication
19: - **Conflict Detection**: Smart conflict detection with baseline checksums
20: 
21: ## Architecture
22: 
23: ```
24: ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
25: │                      Browser (Client)                       │
26: │  ┌─────────────┐  ┌─────────────┐  ┌─────────────────┐   │
27: │  │ Files Tree  │  │   Chat      │  │    Changes      │   │
28: │  │   (Left)    │  │  (Center)   │  │    (Right)      │   │
29: │  └─────────────┘  └─────────────┘  └─────────────────┘   │
30: └─────────────────────────┬─────────────────────────────────┘
31:                           │ WebSocket / HTTP
32: ┌─────────────────────────▼─────────────────────────────────┐
33: │                 mimo-platform (Hono/Bun)                   │
34: │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
35: │  │  Auth  │  Projects  │  Sessions  │  Agents  │ Sync │  │
36: │  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
37: │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
38: │  │              WebSocket Handlers                      │  │
39: │  │         (Chat, Agent Connections)                  │  │
40: │  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
41: └─────────────────────────┬─────────────────────────────────┘
42:                           │
43: ┌─────────────────────────▼─────────────────────────────────┐
44: │                   mimo-agent (Binary)                      │
45: │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
46: │  │         File Watcher  │  ACP Process Proxy        │  │
47: │  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
48: └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
49: ```
50: 
51: ## Installation
52: 
53: ### Prerequisites
54: 
55: - [Bun](https://bun.sh) 1.0+
56: - [Fossil](https://fossil-scm.org) 2.27+
57: - Git (for Git repository support)
58: 
59: ### Quick Start
60: 
61: ```bash
62: # Clone the repository
63: git clone https://github.com/your-org/mimo.git
64: cd mimo
65: 
66: # Install dependencies
67: cd packages/mimo-platform
68: bun install
69: 
70: # Start the server
71: bun run dev
72: ```
73: 
74: The platform will be available at `http://localhost:3000`
75: 
76: ### Build the Agent
77: 
78: ```bash
79: cd packages/mimo-agent
80: bun install
81: bun run build
82: ```
83: 
84: This creates `dist/mimo-agent` which is used by the platform.
85: 
86: ## Usage
87: 
88: ### Public Landing Page
89: 
90: When you first navigate to `http://localhost:3000`, you'll see a public landing page displaying:
91: - Platform overview and features
92: - List of all public projects (names, descriptions, owners, repo types)
93: - Login and Register buttons
94: 
95: Clicking on a project card will redirect you to login if not authenticated, or take you directly to the project detail if authenticated.
96: 
97: ### Authentication
98: 
99: 1. Navigate to `http://localhost:3000/auth/register`
100: 2. Create an account
101: 3. Login at `http://localhost:3000/auth/login`
102: 
103: ### Creating a Project
104: 
105: 1. Click "Create Project" on the projects page
106: 2. Enter project name
107: 3. Add an optional description (recommended ~200 chars, max 500)
108: 4. Provide Git or Fossil repository URL
109: 5. The system imports/clones the repository
110: 
111: ### Starting a Session
112: 
113: 1. Select a project from the projects list
114: 2. Click "New Session"
115: 3. Enter session name
116: 4. The system sets up a Fossil worktree
117: 
118: ### Working with Agents
119: 
120: 1. In a session, click "Start Agent"
121: 2. The platform spawns an agent process
122: 3. Chat with the agent in the center buffer
123: 4. File changes appear in the right buffer automatically
124: 
125: ### Committing Changes
126: 
127: 1. Make changes through the agent
128: 2. Click "Commit" button or press `C-x c`
129: 3. Enter commit message
130: 4. Changes are committed to Fossil and pushed to the original repository
131: 
132: ## Configuration
133: 
134: Configuration is stored in `~/.mimo/config.yaml`:
135: 
136: ```yaml
137: theme: dark
138: fontSize: 14
139: fontFamily: monospace
140: keybindings:
141:   cancel_request: "C-c C-c"
142:   commit: "C-x c"
143:   find_file: "C-x C-f"
144:   switch_project: "C-x p"
145:   switch_session: "C-x s"
146:   focus_left: "C-x h"
147:   focus_center: "C-x j"
148:   focus_right: "C-x l"
149: ```
150: 
151: Edit via the web UI at `/config` or directly in the file.
152: 
153: ## Directory Structure
154: 
155: ```
156: ~/.mimo/
157: ├── config.yaml           # User configuration
158: ├── users/
159: │   └── {username}/
160: │       └── credentials.yaml
161: ├── projects/
162: │   └── {project-id}/
163: │       ├── project.yaml
164: │       ├── repo.fossil
165: │       ├── original/     # Original repo worktree
166: │       └── sessions/
167: │           └── {session-id}/
168: │               ├── session.yaml
169: │               └── chat.jsonl
170: └── agents/
171:     └── {agent-id}/
172:         └── agent.yaml
173: ```
174: 
175: ## Development
176: 
177: ```bash
178: # Run tests
179: bun test
180: 
181: # Run with hot reload
182: bun run dev
183: 
184: # Build for production
185: bun run build
186: ```
````

```
├── config.yaml           # User configuration
├── users/
│   └── {username}/
│       └── credentials.yaml
├── projects/
│   └── {project-id}/
│       ├── project.yaml      # ✓ Created
│       ├── repo.fossil       # ✗ MISSING - Not created
│       ├── original/         # ✗ MISSING - Not created  
│       └── sessions/
│           └── {session-id}/
│               ├── session.yaml  # ✓ Created
│               └── chat.jsonl
│       └── worktrees/
│           └── {session-id}/   # ✓ Directory created but EMPTY
└── agents/
    └── {agent-id}/
        └── agent.yaml
```

## The Problem

Two things are missing:

1. **When creating a project**: The system needs to clone the Git repo, convert it to Fossil, and store the Fossil repo at `repo.fossil`

2. **When creating a session**: The worktree needs to be populated by opening the Fossil repo, not just creating an empty directory

Let me look at what the design docs say about this:

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/mimo-platform/design.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 00:56:22
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/mimo-platform/design.md

````
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/mimo-platform/design.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: # Design: mimo-platform
2: 
3: ## Context
4: 
5: The goal is to build a minimal, Emacs-style web editor for collaborative AI-assisted development. The system avoids databases entirely, using the filesystem as the single source of truth. The architecture uses Fossil as an intermediary layer between original repositories (Git or Fossil) and the agent's worktree, allowing consistent cloning and synchronization regardless of the original VCS.
6: 
7: ### Current State
8: This is a greenfield project with no existing codebase to extend.
9: 
10: ### Constraints
11: - **No database**: Everything stored in YAML/JSONL files
12: - **Single-file agent**: mimo-agent must compile to one Bun executable
13: - **Filesystem-driven**: Projects, sessions, and chat history are directories and files
14: - **Emacs-style UI**: Keyboard-driven, buffers, minimal chrome
15: - **ACP Protocol**: Agent communication via stdio through proxy
16: 
17: ## Goals / Non-Goals
18: 
19: **Goals:**
20: - Build minimal TypeScript/Bun platform with filesystem-based state
21: - Support Git and Fossil repositories seamlessly
22: - One Fossil server per session with auto-assigned ports
23: - Agent persists across disconnects
24: - Emacs-inspired UI with file/chat/changes buffers
25: - Keybindings: C-c C-c to cancel, C-x c to commit
26: 
27: **Non-Goals:**
28: - Multi-user sessions (single user per session)
29: - Conflict auto-resolution (manual only)
30: - Real-time collaborative editing
31: - Email confirmation for auth
32: - React/Vue client-side framework
33: 
34: ## Decisions
35: 
36: ### 1. Fossil as Intermediary Layer
37: **Decision:** Import all repositories (Git or Fossil) into Fossil for session management.
38: 
39: **Rationale:**
40: - Fossil supports both Git import and native operation
41: - Provides consistent HTTP cloning interface for agents
42: - Self-contained with built-in server
43: - Simplifies mimo-agent (always clones from Fossil HTTP)
44: 
45: **Alternative:** Native Git worktrees with Fossil worktree simulation
46: - **Rejected:** Added complexity in mimo-agent to handle different VCS
47: 
48: ### 2. Platform Architecture
49: **Decision:** Build platform using TypeScript/Bun with Hono framework for minimal footprint.
50: 
51: **Rationale:**
52: - Single language stack (TypeScript for both platform and agent)
53: - Fast startup and low memory footprint
54: - Bun built-in WebSocket support
55: - Simple, minimal dependencies
56: 
57: **Framework Decision:** Hono - minimal, fast, works great with Bun, JSX support for server-side rendering
58: 
59: **Alternative:** Phoenix (Elixir)
60: - **Rejected:** Too heavy for this use case, TypeScript provides sufficient concurrency with Bun
61: 
62: ### 3. Filesystem Structure
63: **Decision:** Use YAML for config, JSONL for append-only logs.
64: 
65: ```
66: ~/.mimo/
67: ├── users/<name>/credentials.yaml
68: ├── projects/<id>/
69: │   ├── project.yaml
70: │   └── sessions/<session-id>/
71: │       ├── session.yaml
72: │       ├── chat/messages.jsonl
73: │       ├── repo.fossil
74: │       └── worktree/
75: └── agents/
76:     └── <agent-id>/
77:         └── agent.yaml
78: ```
79: 
80: **Rationale:**
81: - Human-readable for debugging
82: - JSONL allows streaming append without rewriting
83: - Directory structure mirrors domain model
84: 
85: **Alternative:** SQLite single file
86: - **Rejected:** User explicitly wants no database
87: 
88: ### 4. Agent Architecture
89: **Decision:** Single-file Bun executable with embedded ACP SDK.
90: 
91: **Rationale:**
92: - Easy distribution (single binary ~50MB)
93: - TypeScript for type safety
94: - Built-in file watching (Bun.watch)
95: 
96: **Alternative:** Deno compile
97: - **Rejected:** Bun has better npm compatibility for @agentclientprotocol/sdk
98: 
99: ### 5. UI Architecture
100: **Decision:** Server-side rendered HTML using Hono's JSX support.
101: 
102: **Rationale:**
103: - Minimal client-side JavaScript (only for WebSocket and keybindings)
104: - Type-safe templates with TypeScript JSX
105: - No build step for frontend assets
106: - Fast server-side rendering
107: - Emacs-style interface with vanilla JS for interactivity
108: 
109: **UI Library Options:**
110: - **Hono JSX**: Type-safe, server-rendered, minimal
111: - **HTMX**: HTML-over-the-wire, but adds dependency
112: - **Alpine.js**: Lightweight reactivity, but more JS
113: - **Vanilla JS**: Maximum minimalism
114: 
115: **Decision:** Hono JSX for rendering + vanilla JS for WebSocket/keybindings
116: 
117: **Layout:**
118: ```
119: ┌──────────────────────────────┬──────────────────────────────┬──────────────────────────────┐
120: │    File Buffer (Left)        │    Chat Buffer (Center)      │    Changes Buffer (Right)    │
121: │                              │                              │                              │
122: │  src/                        │  user> Add dark mode         │  M src/app.js                │
123: │    app.js [M]                │  agent> I'll help...         │  ? src/new.ts                │
124: │    lib/                      │       [streaming...]         │  D src/old.js                │
125: │      auth.js [M]             │                              │                              │
126: │    styles/                   │  >                           │                              │
127: │                              │                              │                              │
128: ├──────────────────────────────┴──────────────────────────────┴──────────────────────────────┤
129: │ Status: C-c C-c cancel | C-x c commit | C-x C-f find-file | C-x p project | C-x s session  │
130: └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
131: ```
132: 
133: **Keybindings (Configurable):**
134: Default bindings stored in `~/.mimo/config.yaml`:
135: 
136: ```yaml
137: keybindings:
138:   cancel_request: "C-c C-c"
139:   commit: "C-x c"
140:   find_file: "C-x C-f"
141:   switch_project: "C-x p"
142:   switch_session: "C-x s"
143:   focus_left: "C-x h"
144:   focus_center: "C-x j"
145:   focus_right: "C-x l"
146: ```
147: 
148: Users can customize via settings UI or by editing config file.
149: 
150: **Alternative:** Tab-based interface
151: - **Rejected:** Not Emacs-style
152: 
153: ### 6. Authentication
154: **Decision:** Simple BCrypt hashed passwords in YAML, JWT tokens for sessions.
155: 
156: **Rationale:**
157: - No email required (user constraint)
158: - JWT is stateless (no DB session store)
159: - Platform generates token, passes to agent via CLI
160: 
161: ## Risks / Trade-offs
162: 
163: **[Risk]** Fossil server port conflicts
164: → **Mitigation:** Auto-assign from range 8000-9000 with collision detection
165: 
166: **[Risk]** Agent crashes leave orphaned processes
167: → **Mitigation:** Platform monitors WebSocket, kills agent on disconnect; agent kills ACP child on exit
168: 
169: **[Risk]** Large chat histories slow down session load
170: → **Mitigation:** JSONL allows streaming load, pagination for display
171: 
172: **[Risk]** Fossil clone for each session consumes disk
173: → **Mitigation:** Expected behavior, sessions are temporary workspaces
174: 
175: **[Risk]** Conflict detection between agent and original repo
176: → **Mitigation:** Platform shows conflict status, requires manual resolution
177: 
178: **[Trade-off]** No real-time file watching from platform
179: → Platform relies on agent to report changes, slight delay but simpler
180: 
181: ## Migration Plan
182: 
183: Not applicable (greenfield project).
184: 
185: ## Open Questions
186: 
187: 1. Should fossil server use SQLite or in-memory for session repos?
188:    - **Decision:** SQLite for persistence across platform restarts
189: 
190: 2. How to handle agent binary updates?
191:    - **Decision:** Separate download, check version on spawn
192: 
193: 3. Port range exhaustion with many sessions?
194:    - **Decision:** 8000-9000 = 1000 ports, reasonable limit
195: 
196: 4. Chat message format?
197:    - **Decision:** {type: "user"|"agent", content: string, timestamp: ISO8601, metadata?: object}

(End of file - total 197 lines)
</content>
````

## The Missing Pieces

1. **Project Creation** - No code calls `vcs.importGitToFossil()` or `vcs.createFossilRepo()`
   - The `projectRepository.create()` just writes a YAML file
   - The VCS module has `importGitToFossil()` but it's never called!

2. **Session Creation** - `setupSessionWorktree()` tries to open a `repo.fossil` that doesn't exist
   - It swallows the error and continues

3. **Agent Token** - The token you showed has `sessionId` and `projectId` but:
   - `generateAgentToken()` only includes `agentId` and `owner`
   - Something else must be generating these tokens (probably session creation?) 
   
4. **Agent Work Directory** - The agent needs:
   - A worktree path to work in
   - To clone/checkout from the Fossil server

## Questions to Explore

- Where is the token with sessionId/projectId being generated? Let me search for that...
- How does the agent know which session it belongs to?
- Should the platform run a Fossil server per session?
- Or should the agent just work with the worktree directly?

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 00:56:55)

Now I have a complete picture. Let me summarize what I've discovered:

#### Current Architecture Understanding

##### Project Creation Flow
1. User creates a project with `repoUrl` (Git or Fossil URL) and `repoType`
2. `projectRepository.create()` just creates a YAML file with metadata - **NO repository cloning happens**
3. No `repo.fossil` file is created
4. No `original/` directory is created for the original repo worktree

##### Session Creation Flow  
1. User creates a session, assigns an agent
2. `sessionRepository.create()` creates the session YAML and creates worktree directory
3. `vcs.setupSessionWorktree()` is called but fails silently because:
   - It expects `repo.fossil` at `projectPath/repo.fossil`
   - But **this file was never created during project creation**

##### What's Missing

**For Projects:**
1. When a project is created, the system should:
   - Clone the original repository (Git or Fossil)
   - Import it into a Fossil repo (`repo.fossil`)
   - Create an `original/` worktree for the platform to track baseline

**For Sessions:**
1. When a session is created:
   - The worktree should be opened from `repo.fossil`
   - Currently fails because `repo.fossil` doesn't exist

**For Agents:**
1. The token with `sessionId` and `projectId` is being generated somewhere, but `agentService.generateAgentToken()` only creates tokens with `agentId` and `owner`
2. There's no route/handler that creates agent tokens with session context

##### The Token Mystery

The JWT token the user showed has:
- `agentId`: "8d34bc87-fac1-42c0-a0ef-bf61ea7d28f3"
- `sessionId`: "e09c7ebe-8d3a-4226-8f8e-61ca60effaa0"  


- `projectId`: a unique identifier
- `owner`: "jova"

I need to investigate the token generation process carefully. The session ID is present, but the current method of creating tokens doesn't support including session context. This suggests there's an undiscovered mechanism for token generation that I haven't yet located in the existing code.

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 00:57:03)

Now I understand the system better. Let me summarize the key findings:

1. **Project creation** - Creates a directory at `~/.mimo/projects/{project-id}/` with:
   - `project.yaml` (metadata)
   - NO `repo.fossil` file! (this is a bug)
   - NO `original/` directory

2. **Session creation** - Creates:
   - `~/.mimo/projects/{project-id}/sessions/{session-id}/session.yaml`
   - `~/.mimo/projects/{project-id}/worktrees/{session-id}/` directory (empty!)

3. **The problem**: 
   - When a project is created from a Git URL, the system should:
     1. Create a Fossil repo from the Git URL (`importGitToFossil`)
     2. This would create `repo.fossil` and open a worktree in `original/`
   
   - When a session is created:
     1. It tries to open `repo.fossil` in the worktree (`setupSessionWorktree`)
     2. But `repo.fossil` doesn't exist because the import never happened!

4. **Token issue**: 
   - The token the user showed has `sessionId` and `projectId`, but `generateAgentToken` only creates tokens with `agentId` and `owner`.
   - This suggests there's supposed to be a different token generation path that includes session context

Let me check if there's supposed to be a different token for connecting agents to sessions.

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/auth/jwt.ts

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 00:57:06
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/auth/jwt.ts

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/auth/jwt.ts</path>

<content>1: import { SignJWT, jwtVerify } from "jose";
2: 
3: const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || "your-secret-key-change-in-production";
4: const secret = new TextEncoder().encode(JWT_SECRET);
5: 
6: export interface JWTPayload {
7:   username: string;
8:   exp?: number;
9: }
10: 
11: export async function generateToken(
12:   username: string,
13:   expiresIn: string = "7d"
14: ): Promise<string> {
15:   const token = await new SignJWT({ username })
16:     .setProtectedHeader({ alg: "HS256" })
17:     .setIssuedAt()
18:     .setExpirationTime(expiresIn)
19:     .sign(secret);
20:   
21:   return token;
22: }
23: 
24: export async function verifyToken(token: string): Promise<JWTPayload | null> {
25:   try {
26:     const { payload } = await jwtVerify(token, secret);
27:     return {
28:       username: payload.username as string,
29:       exp: payload.exp,
30:     };
31:   } catch {
32:     return null;
33:   }
34: }

(End of file - total 34 lines)
</content>
```

**What happens on Project Creation (projects/routes.tsx:26-69):**

2. Creates project directory
3. Writes `project.yaml`

1. Creates session directory
2. Creates worktree directory
3. Writes `session.yaml`
4. Calls `vcs.setupSessionWorktree()`

```typescript
async generateAgentToken(agent: Agent): Promise<string> {
  const token = await new SignJWT({
    agentId: agent.id,
    owner: agent.owner,
  })
    .setProtectedHeader({ alg: "HS256" })
    .setIssuedAt()
    .setExpirationTime("24h")
    .sign(AGENT_SECRET);

  return token;
}
```

1. The token was generated somewhere else (not using this method)

```typescript
  return await this.openFossil(fossilPath, worktreePath);
}
```

#### Key Disconnects

```typescript
// projects/routes.tsx - line 57
const project = await projectRepository.create({
  repoUrl,  // ← stored and forgotten
  ...
});
// No importGitToFossil() call here!
```

**2. The design says "Fossil server per session" but no server runs:**
> "One Fossil server per session with auto-assigned ports"

```
├── sessions/<id>/   ✓
└── worktrees/<id>/   ✗ EMPTY (should have repo files)
```

#### Questions to Shape the Solution

1. **Do you want the Fossil server approach** (as designed) where:
   - Platform runs Fossil HTTP server per session
   - Agent clones from that HTTP server
   - Agent pushes changes back via HTTP

   **OR a simpler direct filesystem approach** where:
   - Agent works directly in the worktree directory
   - No HTTP server needed
   - Files synchronized via WebSocket messages

2. **How should the agent know where to work?**
   - Token fields (sessionId, projectId, worktreePath)
   - WebSocket handshake message
   - Environment variables / CLI args

3. **When should repository import happen?** 
   - Project creation time (import Git → Fossil once)
   - Session creation time (each session gets its own)
   - On-demand when agent connects

## Open Questions for Exploration

1. **Session-scoped vs Project-scoped Fossil repo:**

#### Questions Before We Exit Explore Mode

**1. Agent-session relationship:**

Looking at your `agent.yaml`, I see:
```yaml
sessionId: e09c7ebe-...
projectId: 7387445d-...
```

Is this **1:1** (one agent = one session) or **1:many** (one agent can work on multiple sessions)?

This affects:
- Token: does it include a single `sessionId` or an array?
- API: `GET /api/agents/me/sessions` returns one or many?
- WebSocket: how does agent know which session to report changes for?

**2. Fossil server lifecycle:**

```
Session Created → Server Started → ... → Session Deleted → Server Stopped?
```

Or:

```
Agent Connects → Server Started → Agent Disconnects → Server Stopped?
```

The README says:
> "One Fossil server per session with auto-assigned ports"

This implies server starts on session creation. But if no agent is assigned, it's wasteful. What's the expected lifecycle?

**3. Worktree sync strategy:**

The platform has `worktree/` inside the session. The agent also clones to its local directory. How should these sync?

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  Option A: Platform is source of truth                       │
│    Agent watches local → sends changes → platform applies    │
│    Platform is canonical worktree                            │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  Option B: Agent is source of truth                          │
│    Agent makes changes locally                               │
│    Platform worktree is just for merging/conflict detection │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  Option C: Both are equal peers                              │
│    Bi-directional sync with conflict detection              │
│    Changes flow both ways via Fossil commits                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

Looking at `sync/service.ts`, I see it's tracking `baselineChecksums` and `originalRepoPath`, suggesting **Option A** (platform is truth, agent reports changes).

**4. The "original" repository:**

The README and design mention:
```
│   ├── repo.fossil
│   ├── original/     # Original repo worktree  ← What is this for?
│   └── sessions/
```

What's the purpose of `original/`? Is it:
- A cached checkout of the upstream for diff comparison?
- The agent's local copy?

**Flow:**

```
SESSION CREATION:
  1. Clone URL → upstream/
     (git clone or fossil clone, depending on repoType)
  
  2. Import to fossil → repo.fossil
     fossil import --git upstream/.git repo.fossil   (if git)
     fossil clone upstream/.fossil repo.fossil        (if fossil)

AGENT WORKS:

USER COMMITS:
  7. Commit in fossil (repo.fossil)
  8. Sync to upstream: fossil export back to upstream/
  9. Push upstream/ to remote origin
```

**Question:** For step 2, is `repo.fossil` a **one-time import** from upstream, or does it need to **stay synced** with upstream (bi-directional)?

Meaning:
- If upstream changes (user pulls new commits), should repo.fossil get them?
- Or is repo.fossil isolated after import, and only syncs on commit?

## User (2026-04-04 01:07:35)

one time

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 01:07:37)

Now I have a complete picture. Let me document this clearly:

1. Session creation:
   - Clone URL → upstream/ (git or fossil)
   - Import to fossil → repo.fossil (one-time copy)
   - repo.fossil is the fossil proxy

2. Agent connects:
   - Start fossil server for repo.fossil
   - Agent clones from fossil server to local workdir

3. Agent works:
   - Watches files, sends changes
   - Platform applies to repo.fossil checkout

4. User commits:
   - Commit to repo.fossil
   - Export to upstream/
   - Push upstream to remote

This is clean. I should summarize the complete architecture now.
## Agent (2026-04-04 01:07:38)

Crystal clear. Here's the final architecture:

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                         FINAL ARCHITECTURE                                   │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                             │
│  SESSION CREATION:                                                           │
│    1. Clone URL → upstream/  (git clone OR fossil clone)                   │
│    2. Import to fossil → repo.fossil (one-time, isolated)                  │
│    3. Open: fossil open repo.fossil checkout/  ← NEW: not "worktree"!     │
│                                                                             │
│  SESSION DIRECTORY:                                                          │
│    sessions/<session-id>/                                                    │
│    ├── session.yaml           ← agentIds, port, status                      │
│    ├── upstream/              ← original repo (git/fossil)                 │
│    │   └── .git / .fossil                                                   │
│    ├── repo.fossil            ← fossil proxy (one-time copy)               │
│    └── checkout/              ← where platform applies agent changes       │
│                                                                             │
│  AGENT FLOW:                                                                 │
│    Connect (WS, token {agentId, owner})                                     │
│    → GET /api/agents/me/sessions                                            │
│    → For each session:                                                      │
│       ← Platform starts fossil server (port)                               │
│       ← Platform sends "session_ready" {port, sessionId}                   │
│       → Agent: fossil clone http://platform:port workdir                   │
│       → Agent watches workdir, sends "file_changed"                       │
│       → Platform applies to checkout/                                       │
│                                                                             │
│  COMMIT FLOW:                                                                │
│    User clicks Commit → Platform:                                            │
│       1. Commit in checkout/ (via fossil)                                  │
│       2. Export to upstream/: fossil export --git . → upstream/            │
│       3. Push upstream/ to remote origin                                    │
│                                                                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

## Summary of All Changes Needed

| Component | Change |
|-----------|--------|
| **Token** | `{agentId, owner}` only, remove sessionId/projectId |
| **Agent YAML** | `sessionIds: []` (array, not single sessionId) |
| **API** | Add `GET /api/agents/me/sessions` |
| **Session creation** | Clone URL → upstream/, import → repo.fossil, open → checkout/ |
| **Session directory** | `worktree/` → `checkout/`, add `upstream/` |
| **Fossil server** | Start on agent connect, stop on disconnect, track port |
| **Agent WebSocket** | Receive "session_ready" messages, know which port for each session |
| **Agent bootstrap** | `fossil clone http://platform:port` to get initial files |
| **File sync** | Agent sends changes → Platform applies to checkout/ |
| **Commit** | Commit in fossil → export to upstream → push to remote |

Ready to implement. Use `/opsx:new` to create a change or `/opsx:ff` to fast-forward.

1. Create a proposal that outlines WHY this change is needed
2. Be specific about what changes

The main changes needed:
1. Session creation needs to clone repo to upstream/, import to repo.fossil, and open checkout/
2. Agent token should only include {agentId, owner}, not sessionId/projectId
3. Agent YAML should have sessionIds array instead of single sessionId
