### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/session-repo-import/proposal.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:08:12
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/session-repo-import/proposal.md
content: # Proposal: session-repo-import

## Why

Session creation currently creates empty worktrees without actual repository files. Agents cannot bootstrap their workspace because there's no Fossil server to clone from, and the synchronization architecture between platform and agent is not implemented. This change enables the complete session lifecycle: repository import, agent bootstrap, and bidirectional file synchronization.

## What Changes

- **Session Creation**: Clone repository to `upstream/`, import to `repo.fossil`, open fossil checkout to `checkout/`
- **Token Generation**: Remove sessionId/projectId from agent tokens; tokens only contain `{agentId, owner}`
- **Agent Repository**: Change single `sessionId` to `sessionIds` array in agent.yaml
- **API Endpoint**: Add `GET /api/agents/me/sessions` for agents to fetch assigned sessions
- **Fossil Server**: Start HTTP server per assigned session on agent connect, stop on disconnect
- **WebSocket Protocol**: Add `session_ready` message from platform to agent with port assignment
- **Agent Bootstrap**: Agent receives ports, clones from Fossil HTTP server to local workdir
- **File Sync**: Platform applies agent-reported changes to `checkout/` directory
- **Commit Flow**: Commit in fossil → export to upstream → push to remote origin
- **Directory Structure**: Rename `worktree/` to `checkout/`, add `upstream/` directory

## Capabilities

### New Capabilities

- `fossil-server`: Per-session Fossil HTTP server lifecycle management with dynamic port assignment
- `session-bootstrap`: Repository cloning, fossil import, and checkout creation during session creation
- `agent-sessions-api`: REST API for agents to discover assigned sessions with Fossil server ports

### Modified Capabilities

- `agent-lifecycle`: Token generation removes session-scoped claims; agents fetch sessions via API instead of receiving in token
- `file-sync`: Platform applies changes to `checkout/` directory instead of `worktree/`
- `session-management`: Session creation now includes repository import and checkout; adds `upstream/` and `checkout/` directories

## Impact

- **Affected Code**: 
  - `sessions/repository.ts`: Add directory creation for `upstream/` and `checkout/`
  - `sessions/routes.tsx`: Add VCS operations on session creation
  - `agents/service.ts`: Modify token generation, remove sessionId/projectId
  - `agents/repository.ts`: Change sessionId to sessionIds array
  - `vcs/index.ts`: Add Fossil HTTP server management methods
  - New API route: `GET /api/agents/me/sessions`
  - WebSocket handler: Add `session_ready` message type
  
- **Affected Storage**:
  - `sessions/<id>/session.yaml`: Add `port` field
  - `agents/<id>/agent.yaml`: Change `sessionId` to `sessionIds`
  
- **Dependencies**: Fossil SCM must be installed on platform server
  
- **Network**: Fossil HTTP servers on ports 8000-9000 per session

```

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 01:08:30)

Now I'll create the specs for the new capabilities following the template format.

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/session-repo-import/specs/fossil-server/spec.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:08:33
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/session-repo-import/specs/fossil-server/spec.md
content: ## ADDED Requirements

### Requirement: Platform starts Fossil HTTP server when agent connects

The platform SHALL start a Fossil HTTP server for each session assigned to the connecting agent. 

#### Scenario: Agent connects with assigned sessions
- **WHEN** agent sends WebSocket message `agent_ready` with valid token
- **THEN** platform starts Fossil HTTP server for each assigned session
- **AND** platform assigns an available port from range 8000-9000
- **AND** platform stores the port in session.yaml
- **AND** platform sends `session_ready` message to agent with `{sessionId, port}`

#### Scenario: No assigned sessions
- **WHEN** agent connects with no assigned sessions
- **THEN** platform sends empty `session_ready` array
- **AND** no Fossil servers are started

### Requirement: Platform assigns unique ports for Fossil servers

The platform SHALL assign ports from range 8000-9000 with collision detection.

#### Scenario: Port assignment with available ports
- **WHEN** platform needs to start Fossil server
- **THEN** platform finds first available port in range 8000-9000
- **AND** platform marks port as in-use
- **AND** platform starts Fossil server on assigned port

#### Scenario: Port exhaustion
- **WHEN** all ports 8000-9000 are in use
- **THEN** platform returns error `PORTS_EXHAUSTED`
- **AND** session is marked as `error` state

### Requirement: Platform stops Fossil server when agent disconnects

The platform SHALL stop Fossil HTTP servers for all sessions assigned to the disconnecting agent.

#### Scenario: Agent disconnects gracefully
- **WHEN** agent WebSocket closes normally
- **THEN** platform stops Fossil servers for all assigned sessions
- **AND** platform releases assigned ports
- **AND** platform marks sessions as `paused`

#### Scenario: Agent connection lost
- **WHEN** agent WebSocket closes unexpectedly or times out
- **THEN** platform stops Fossil servers after 30-second grace period
- **AND** platform releases assigned ports
- **AND** platform marks sessions as `paused`

### Requirement: Fossil server serves repository for agent clone

The Fossil server SHALL serve the session's `repo.fossil` for agent cloning.

#### Scenario: Agent clones from Fossil server
- **WHEN** agent sends `fossil clone http://platform:port` request
- **THEN** Fossil server responds with repository data
- **AND** agent receives complete repository clone

```

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 01:08:36)

Now create specs for session-bootstrap.

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/session-repo-import/specs/session-bootstrap/spec.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:08:40
**Parameters:**
content: ## ADDED Requirements

### Requirement: Session creation clones repository to upstream

The platform SHALL clone the project's repository URL to the `upstream/` directory during session creation.

#### Scenario: Clone Git repository
- **WHEN** project has `repoType: "git"` and valid Git URL
- **THEN** platform executes `git clone <repoUrl> upstream/` in session directory
- **AND** upstream directory contains `.git` folder
- **AND** platform creates `upstream/` directory

#### Scenario: Clone Fossil repository
- **WHEN** project has `repoType: "fossil"` and valid Fossil URL
- **THEN** platform executes `fossil clone <repoUrl> upstream/.fossil` 
- **AND** platform executes `fossil open upstream/.fossil` in `upstream/` directory
- **AND** platform creates `upstream/` directory

#### Scenario: Clone failure
- **WHEN** repository clone fails (invalid URL, auth required, network error)
- **THEN** session creation returns error `CLONE_FAILED`
- **AND** session is not created
- **AND** error message includes failure reason

### Requirement: Session creation imports repository to Fossil proxy

The platform SHALL import the upstream repository into `repo.fossil` as a one-time copy.

#### Scenario: Import from Git upstream
- **WHEN** upstream is a Git repository
- **THEN** platform executes `fossil import --git upstream/.git repo.fossil`
- **AND** `repo.fossil` is created in session directory
- **AND** imported repository contains all commits from upstream

#### Scenario: Import from Fossil upstream
- **WHEN** upstream is a Fossil repository
- **THEN** platform executes `fossil clone upstream/.fossil repo.fossil`
- **AND** `repo.fossil` is created in session directory

#### Scenario: Import failure
- **WHEN** fossil import fails
- **THEN** session creation returns error `IMPORT_FAILED`
- **AND** session is not created

### Requirement: Session creation opens Fossil checkout

The platform SHALL open the Fossil repository into `checkout/` directory.

#### Scenario: Open checkout
- **WHEN** `repo.fossil` exists after import
- **THEN** platform executes `fossil open repo.fossil checkout/`
- **AND** `checkout/` directory contains working copy of all files
- **AND** session can be used for file synchronization

#### Scenario: Open failure
- **WHEN** checkout open fails
- **THEN** session creation returns error `CHECKOUT_FAILED`
- **AND** session is not created

### Requirement: Session directory structure

The platform SHALL create the complete session directory structure.

#### Scenario: Complete session structure
- **WHEN** session creation succeeds
- **THEN** session directory contains:
  - `session.yaml`: session metadata
  - `upstream/`: original repository (git or fossil)
  - `repo.fossil`: fossil proxy copy
  - `checkout/`: working copy for platform changes
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/session-repo-import/specs/session-bootstrap/spec.md

```

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 01:08:42)

Now create the agent-sessions-api spec.

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/session-repo-import/specs/agent-sessions-api/spec.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:08:44
**Parameters:**
content: ## ADDED Requirements

### Requirement: Agent can fetch assigned sessions

The platform SHALL provide an API endpoint for agents to retrieve their assigned sessions.

#### Scenario: Fetch sessions with valid token
- **WHEN** agent sends `GET /api/agents/me/sessions` with valid JWT token in Authorization header
- **THEN** platform returns array of session objects
- **AND** each session object includes `sessionId`, `projectId`, `sessionName`, `status`, `port`
- **AND** only sessions assigned to this agent are returned

#### Scenario: Fetch sessions without token
- **WHEN** agent sends `GET /api/agents/me/sessions` without Authorization header
- **THEN** platform returns `401 Unauthorized`
- **AND** response body contains `{"error": "Missing token"}`

#### Scenario: Fetch sessions with invalid token
- **WHEN** agent sends `GET /api/agents/me/sessions` with invalid JWT token
- **THEN** platform returns `401 Unauthorized`
- **AND** response body contains `{"error": "Invalid token"}`

#### Scenario: No assigned sessions
- **WHEN** agent has no sessions assigned
- **THEN** platform returns empty array `[]`
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/session-repo-import/specs/agent-sessions-api/spec.md

```

+
+### Requirement: Agent can fetch assigned sessions
+
+The platform SHALL provide an API endpoint for agents to retrieve their assigned sessions.
+
+#### Scenario: Fetch sessions with valid token
+- **WHEN** agent sends `GET /api/agents/me/sessions` with valid JWT token in Authorization header
+- **THEN** platform returns array of session objects
+- **AND** each session object includes `sessionId`, `projectId`, `sessionName`, `status`, `port`
+- **AND** only sessions assigned to this agent are returned
+
+#### Scenario: Fetch sessions without token
+- **WHEN** agent sends `GET /api/agents/me/sessions` without Authorization header
+- **THEN** platform returns `401 Unauthorized`
+- **AND** response body contains `{"error": "Missing token"}`
+
+#### Scenario: Fetch sessions with invalid token
+- **WHEN** agent sends `GET /api/agents/me/sessions` with invalid JWT token
+- **THEN** platform returns `401 Unauthorized`
+- **AND** response body contains `{"error": "Invalid token"}`
+
+#### Scenario: No assigned sessions
+- **WHEN** agent has no sessions assigned
+- **THEN** platform returns empty array `[]`

<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## ADDED Requirements
2: 
3: ### Requirement: User can create an agent
4: The system SHALL allow users to create agents for sessions. Creating an agent generates a token and spawns mimo-agent process.
5: 
6: #### Scenario: Create agent for session
7: - **WHEN** authenticated user creates agent for session "fix-auth-bug"
8: - **THEN** system generates JWT token {session_id: "...", exp: "..."}
9: - **AND** system spawns mimo-agent process with --token=<jwt> --platform=ws://localhost:4000/agent
10: - **AND** system stores agent.yaml with {token: "...", session_id: "...", status: "starting"}
11: - **AND** system displays "Agent starting..." in chat buffer
12: 
13: #### Scenario: Agent connects successfully
14: - **WHEN** mimo-agent connects via WebSocket with valid token
15: - **THEN** system updates agent.yaml status to "connected"
16: - **AND** system appends "Agent connected" to chat buffer
17: 
18: #### Scenario: Agent fails to start
19: - **WHEN** mimo-agent executable not found or crashes
20: - **THEN** system updates agent.yaml status to "failed"
21: - **AND** system displays error message in chat buffer
22: - **AND** system allows retry
23: 
24: ### Requirement: User can list active agents
25: The system SHALL display running agents for the current user.
26: 
27: #### Scenario: List active agents
28: - **WHEN** user navigates to agents page
29: - **THEN** system displays all agents with status: session name, status, pid, started_at
30: 
31: #### Scenario: Filter by status
32: - **WHEN** user filters agents by "connected" status
33: - **THEN** system displays only agents with status "connected"
34: 
35: ### Requirement: System can cancel current ACP request
36: The system SHALL allow users to cancel the current ACP agent request.
37: 
38: #### Scenario: Cancel current request with C-c C-c
39: - **WHEN** user presses C-c C-c in session
40: - **THEN** system sends cancel signal to current ACP request
41: - **AND** system appends "Request cancelled" to chat buffer
42: - **AND** agent remains connected and ready for next request
43: 
44: #### Scenario: Cancel when no active request
45: - **WHEN** user presses C-c C-c with no active ACP request
46: - **THEN** system displays "No active request to cancel"
47: 
48: ### Requirement: System can terminate agent
49: The system SHALL allow users to kill the entire agent process.
50: 
51: #### Scenario: Kill agent via command
52: - **WHEN** user executes kill-agent command
53: - **THEN** system terminates mimo-agent process
54: - **AND** system kills ACP child process
55: - **AND** system updates agent.yaml status to "killed"
56: - **AND** system appends "Agent terminated" to chat buffer
57: 
58: #### Scenario: Agent process dies unexpectedly
59: - **WHEN** mimo-agent process exits unexpectedly
60: - **THEN** system detects via WebSocket disconnect
61: - **AND** system kills any orphaned ACP process
62: - **AND** system updates agent.yaml status to "died"
63: 
64: ### Requirement: Agent persists across disconnects
65: The system SHALL maintain agent process when user disconnects.
66: 
67: #### Scenario: Agent continues after disconnect
68: - **WHEN** user disconnects from session
69: - **THEN** mimo-agent process continues running
70: - **AND** agent continues working on assigned tasks
71: 
72: #### Scenario: Agent reports changes after reconnect
73: - **WHEN** user reconnects after agent made file changes
74: - **THEN** system receives buffered change notifications
75: - **AND** system updates file tree with changes
76: 
77: ### Requirement: Agent uses token for authentication
78: The system SHALL validate JWT tokens from agents.
79: 
80: #### Scenario: Valid token authentication
81: - **WHEN** agent connects with valid JWT token
82: - **THEN** system identifies session from token claims
83: - **AND** system authorizes WebSocket connection
84: 
85: #### Scenario: Invalid token rejection
86: - **WHEN** agent connects with invalid or expired token
87: - **THEN** system rejects WebSocket connection
88: - **AND** system logs authentication failure

(End of file - total 88 lines)

<content>1: ## ADDED Requirements
2: 
3: ### Requirement: Agent reports file changes to platform
4: The system SHALL receive file change notifications from mimo-agent.
5: 
6: #### Scenario: Single file change
7: - **WHEN** agent modifies file "src/app.js"
8: - **THEN** mimo-agent sends WebSocket message: {type: "file_changed", files: ["src/app.js"]}
9: - **AND** platform marks file with [M] indicator
10: 
11: #### Scenario: Multiple file changes
12: - **WHEN** agent modifies multiple files
13: - **THEN** mimo-agent sends single message with all changed files
14: - **AND** platform updates all file indicators
15: 
16: #### Scenario: New file created
17: - **WHEN** agent creates new file "src/new.ts"
18: - **THEN** mimo-agent sends message: {type: "file_changed", files: ["src/new.ts"], is_new: true}
19: - **AND** platform marks file with [?] indicator
20: 
21: ### Requirement: Platform synchronizes changes to original repository
22: The system SHALL copy changed files from agent worktree to original repository worktree.
23: 
24: #### Scenario: Sync modified file
25: - **WHEN** platform receives file change notification
26: - **THEN** system copies file from session worktree to original repo worktree
27: - **AND** system preserves file permissions
28: 
29: #### Scenario: Sync new file
30: - **WHEN** platform receives new file notification
31: - **THEN** system copies file and creates parent directories if needed
32: - **AND** system preserves file permissions
33: 
34: #### Scenario: Batch sync on reconnect
35: - **WHEN** user reconnects after offline period
36: - **THEN** system receives all buffered file changes
37: - **AND** system syncs all files to original repo worktree
38: 
39: ### Requirement: Platform detects conflicts
40: The system SHALL identify when agent changes conflict with original repository changes.
41: 
42: #### Scenario: Conflict detection
43: - **WHEN** platform attempts sync and detects file was modified in original repo
44: - **THEN** system marks file with conflict indicator [!]
45: - **AND** system displays "Conflicts detected" in changes buffer
46: - **AND** system requires manual resolution
47: 
48: #### Scenario: Show conflict details
49: - **WHEN** user clicks conflicted file
50: - **THEN** system displays diff between agent version and original repo version
51: 
52: ### Requirement: Platform handles file deletions
53: The system SHALL detect and sync file deletions.
54: 
55: #### Scenario: File deleted by agent
56: - **WHEN** agent deletes file "src/old.js"
57: - **THEN** mimo-agent sends message: {type: "file_changed", files: ["src/old.js"], deleted: true}
58: - **AND** platform marks file with [D] indicator
59: - **AND** system removes file from original repo worktree
60: 
61: ### Requirement: File sync is bidirectional
62: The system SHALL support manual sync from original repo to session.
63: 
64: #### Scenario: Pull latest changes
65: - **WHEN** user requests sync from original repo
66: - **THEN** system copies changes from original repo to session worktree
67: - **AND** system updates file tree indicators
68: - **AND** system notifies agent of changes
69: 
70: #### Scenario: Sync conflicts with agent changes
71: - **WHEN** pull conflicts with uncommitted agent changes
72: - **THEN** system displays conflict warning
73: - **AND** system requires manual resolution

(End of file - total 73 lines)
</content>
```


### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/mimo-platform/specs/session-management/spec.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:08:51
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/mimo-platform/specs/session-management/spec.md

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/mimo-platform/specs/session-management/spec.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## ADDED Requirements
2: 
3: ### Requirement: User can create a session
4: The system SHALL allow users to create sessions within a project. Each session creates a worktree and starts a Fossil server.
5: 
6: #### Scenario: Create session with title
7: - **WHEN** authenticated user submits session title "fix-auth-bug" for project "my-app"
8: - **THEN** system creates directory ~/.mimo/projects/my-app/sessions/fix-auth-bug/
9: - **AND** system clones project's repository to repo.fossil
10: - **AND** system assigns auto-generated port (8000-9000 range)
11: - **AND** system starts Fossil server on assigned port
12: - **AND** system stores session.yaml with {title: "fix-auth-bug", port: <assigned>, status: "active"}
13: - **AND** system displays session view
14: 
15: #### Scenario: Port collision handling
16: - **WHEN** system attempts to start Fossil server on occupied port
17: - **THEN** system tries next available port in range
18: - **AND** system continues until successful
19: 
20: #### Scenario: Duplicate session title
21: - **WHEN** user submits session title that already exists in project
22: - **THEN** system appends timestamp to title or returns error
23: 
24: ### Requirement: Session persists across disconnects
25: The system SHALL maintain session state when user disconnects.
26: 
27: #### Scenario: Reconnect to active session
28: - **WHEN** user reconnects to existing session
29: - **THEN** system loads chat history from messages.jsonl
30: - **AND** system reattaches to running agent if exists
31: - **AND** system displays current file tree state
32: 
33: #### Scenario: Agent running on reconnect
34: - **WHEN** user reconnects and agent is still running
35: - **THEN** system establishes WebSocket to agent
36: - **AND** system resumes chat stream
37: 
38: ### Requirement: User can delete a session
39: The system SHALL allow users to remove sessions.
40: 
41: #### Scenario: Delete session with cleanup
42: - **WHEN** authenticated user deletes session "fix-auth-bug"
43: - **THEN** system terminates agent process if running
44: - **AND** system stops Fossil server
45: - **AND** system removes ~/.mimo/projects/my-app/sessions/fix-auth-bug/ directory
46: 
47: ### Requirement: Chat messages are stored persistently
48: The system SHALL store chat history in append-only JSONL format.
49: 
50: #### Scenario: Store user message
51: - **WHEN** user sends message "Add dark mode"
52: - **THEN** system appends to messages.jsonl: {type: "user", content: "Add dark mode", timestamp: "..."}
53: 
54: #### Scenario: Store agent message
55: - **WHEN** agent sends response "I'll help with that..."
56: - **THEN** system appends to messages.jsonl: {type: "agent", content: "...", timestamp: "..."}
57: 
58: #### Scenario: Stream agent response
59: - **WHEN** agent streams response in chunks
60: - **THEN** system buffers and stores complete message on finish
61: - **AND** system displays streaming updates via WebSocket
62: 
63: ### Requirement: Session shows file tree with change indicators
64: The system SHALL display project file tree with modification markers in the left buffer.
65: 
66: #### Scenario: Show modified files
67: - **WHEN** agent reports file changes
68: - **THEN** system marks files with [M] in file tree (left buffer)
69: - **AND** system updates changes buffer (right buffer)
70: 
71: #### Scenario: Show new files
72: - **WHEN** agent creates new files
73: - **THEN** system marks files with [?] in file tree (left buffer)
74: 
75: ### Requirement: Session shows file diffs with syntax highlighting
76: The system SHALL display file changes with language-appropriate syntax highlighting.
77: 
78: #### Scenario: View file diff
79: - **WHEN** user clicks on modified file
80: - **THEN** system displays diff with syntax highlighting
81: - **AND** system shows line additions and deletions
82: 
83: ### Requirement: User can navigate file tree
84: The system SHALL allow users to browse and open files.
85: 
86: #### Scenario: Find file
87: - **WHEN** user presses the configured keybinding for find_file
88: - **THEN** system prompts for file path
89: - **AND** system opens file in file buffer
90: 
91: #### Scenario: Click file in tree
92: - **WHEN** user clicks file in file tree
93: - **THEN** system loads file content into file buffer
94: 
95: ### Requirement: Keybindings are configurable
96: The system SHALL allow users to customize keybindings stored in ~/.mimo/config.yaml.
97: 
98: #### Scenario: Load custom keybindings
99: - **WHEN** user starts platform
100: - **THEN** system reads ~/.mimo/config.yaml
101: - **AND** system loads custom keybindings if defined
102: - **AND** system uses defaults for missing bindings
103: 
104: #### Scenario: Use default keybinding
105: - **WHEN** user presses C-c C-c (default cancel)
106: - **THEN** system executes cancel agent command
107: - **AND** keybinding is configurable via config.yaml
108: 
109: #### Scenario: Focus buffer with keybinding
110: - **WHEN** user presses C-x h
111: - **THEN** system focuses file buffer (left)
112: - **AND** system updates active buffer indicator
113: 
114: #### Scenario: Focus chat buffer
115: - **WHEN** user presses C-x j
116: - **THEN** system focuses chat buffer (center)
117: - **AND** system updates active buffer indicator
118: 
119: #### Scenario: Focus changes buffer
120: - **WHEN** user presses C-x l
121: - **THEN** system focuses changes buffer (right)
122: - **AND** system updates active buffer indicator

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/session-repo-import/specs/agent-lifecycle/spec.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:09:03
**Parameters:**
content: ## MODIFIED Requirements

### Requirement: Agent uses token for authentication

The system SHALL validate JWT tokens from agents. Token SHALL contain only `{agentId, owner}` claims.

#### Scenario: Valid token authentication
- **WHEN** agent connects with valid JWT token containing `{agentId, owner}`
- **THEN** system identifies agent from token claims
- **AND** system authorizes WebSocket connection
- **AND** agent fetches assigned sessions via `GET /api/agents/me/sessions`

#### Scenario: Invalid token rejection
- **WHEN** agent connects with invalid or expired token
- **THEN** system rejects WebSocket connection
- **AND** system logs authentication failure

#### Scenario: Token without agentId
- **WHEN** token is missing `agentId` claim
- **THEN** system rejects connection with error `INVALID_TOKEN`

### Requirement: Agent can work on multiple sessions

The system SHALL support one agent working on multiple sessions simultaneously.

#### Scenario: Agent assigned to multiple sessions
- **WHEN** agent.yaml contains `sessionIds: ["session1", "session2"]`
- **THEN** agent receives all sessions from `GET /api/agents/me/sessions`
- **AND** platform starts Fossil servers for all assigned sessions
- **AND** agent can clone and work on all sessions

#### Scenario: Assign session to agent
- **WHEN** user assigns session "fix-auth-bug" to agent "agent-123"
- **THEN** system appends sessionId to agent.yaml `sessionIds` array
- **AND** session.yaml `assignedAgentId` is set to "agent-123"

#### Scenario: Unassign session from agent
- **WHEN** user unassigns session from agent
- **THEN** system removes sessionId from agent.yaml `sessionIds` array
- **AND** session.yaml `assignedAgentId` is set to null

### Requirement: Agent persists across disconnects

The system SHALL maintain agent process when user disconnects.

#### Scenario: Agent continues after disconnect
- **WHEN** user disconnects from session
- **THEN** mimo-agent process continues running
- **AND** agent continues working on assigned tasks

#### Scenario: Agent reports changes after reconnect
- **WHEN** user reconnects after agent made file changes
- **THEN** system receives buffered change notifications
- **AND** system updates file tree with changes
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/session-repo-import/specs/agent-lifecycle/spec.md

Now I'll create the file-sync modified spec. The key change is that the platform applies changes to `checkout/` instead of `worktree/`.

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/session-repo-import/specs/file-sync/spec.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:09:07
**Parameters:**
content: ## MODIFIED Requirements

### Requirement: Platform synchronizes changes to checkout directory

The system SHALL copy changed files from agent workdir to session's `checkout/` directory.

#### Scenario: Sync modified file
- **WHEN** platform receives file change notification
- **THEN** system copies file from agent workdir to session `checkout/` directory
- **AND** system preserves file permissions
- **AND** system updates file status indicators

#### Scenario: Sync new file
- **WHEN** platform receives new file notification
- **THEN** system copies file to `checkout/` and creates parent directories if needed
- **AND** system preserves file permissions

#### Scenario: Batch sync on reconnect
- **WHEN** user reconnects after offline period
- **THEN** system receives all buffered file changes
- **AND** system syncs all files to `checkout/` directory

### Requirement: Agent reports file changes to platform

The system SHALL receive file change notifications from mimo-agent via WebSocket.

#### Scenario: Single file change
- **WHEN** agent modifies file "src/app.js" in local workdir
- **THEN** mimo-agent sends WebSocket message: `{type: "file_changed", sessionId: "...", files: [{path: "src/app.js", status: "modified"}]}`
- **AND** platform applies change to `checkout/`
- **AND** platform marks file with [M] indicator

#### Scenario: Multiple file changes
- **WHEN** agent modifies multiple files
- **THEN** mimo-agent sends single message with all changed files
- **AND** platform updates all file indicators in `checkout/`

#### Scenario: New file created
- **WHEN** agent creates new file "src/new.ts" in local workdir
- **THEN** mimo-agent sends message: `{type: "file_changed", sessionId: "...", files: [{path: "src/new.ts", status: "new"}]}`
- **AND** platform copies file to `checkout/`
- **AND** platform marks file with [?] indicator
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/session-repo-import/specs/file-sync/spec.md

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 01:09:18)

Now I need to write the modified session-management spec. It needs to reflect that session creation now clones the repository to upstream/, creates repo.fossil, and opens checkout/ instead of worktree/.

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/session-repo-import/specs/session-management/spec.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:09:23
**Parameters:**
content: ## MODIFIED Requirements

### Requirement: User can create a session

The system SHALL allow users to create sessions within a project. Each session clones the repository, creates Fossil proxy, and prepares checkout directory.

#### Scenario: Create session with title
- **WHEN** authenticated user submits session title "fix-auth-bug" for project "my-app"
- **THEN** system creates directory `~/.mimo/projects/<project-id>/sessions/<session-id>/`
- **AND** system clones repository URL to `upstream/` directory
- **AND** system imports to Fossil: `repo.fossil` (one-time copy)
- **AND** system opens Fossil checkout to `checkout/` directory
- **AND** system stores session.yaml with `{name: "fix-auth-bug", status: "active"}`
- **AND** system displays session view

#### Scenario: Clone from Git repository
- **WHEN** project has `repoType: "git"`
- **THEN** system executes `git clone <repoUrl> upstream/`
- **AND** system executes `fossil import --git upstream/.git repo.fossil`
- **AND** system executes `fossil open repo.fossil checkout/`

#### Scenario: Clone from Fossil repository
- **WHEN** project has `repoType: "fossil"`
- **THEN** system executes `fossil clone <repoUrl> upstream/.fossil`
- **AND** system executes `fossil clone upstream/.fossil repo.fossil`
- **AND** system executes `fossil open repo.fossil checkout/`

#### Scenario: Clone failure
- **WHEN** repository clone fails (invalid URL, auth required, network error)
- **THEN** system returns error `CLONE_FAILED`
- **AND** session is not created

#### Scenario: Import failure
- **WHEN** Fossil import fails
- **THEN** system returns error `IMPORT_FAILED`
- **AND** session is not created

#### Scenario: Duplicate session title
- **WHEN** user submits session title that already exists in project
- **THEN** system returns error `SESSION_EXISTS`

### Requirement: Session directory structure

The system SHALL maintain complete session directory structure.

#### Scenario: Complete session structure
- **WHEN** session creation succeeds
- **THEN** session directory contains:
  - `session.yaml`: session metadata `{id, name, projectId, owner, assignedAgentId, status, port, createdAt, updatedAt}`
  - `upstream/`: original repository (git or fossil)
  - `repo.fossil`: Fossil proxy (one-time copy)
  - `checkout/`: working copy for platform changes

### Requirement: User can delete a session

The system SHALL allow users to remove sessions with full cleanup.

#### Scenario: Delete session with cleanup
- **WHEN** authenticated user deletes session "fix-auth-bug"
- **THEN** system terminates agent process if running
- **AND** system stops Fossil server if running
- **AND** system removes entire session directory including `upstream/`, `repo.fossil`, `checkout/`

## ADDED Requirements

### Requirement: Platform starts Fossil server when agent connects

The system SHALL start Fossil HTTP server on agent WebSocket connection for each assigned session.

#### Scenario: Agent connects to session
- **WHEN** agent connects via WebSocket with valid token
- **AND** agent fetches assigned sessions via `GET /api/agents/me/sessions`
- **THEN** platform starts Fossil server for each assigned session
- **AND** platform assigns port 8000-9000
- **AND** platform sends `session_ready` message to agent with `{sessionId, port}`

#### Scenario: Agent disconnects
- **WHEN** agent WebSocket closes
- **THEN** platform stops Fossil servers for all assigned sessions
- **AND** platform releases assigned ports
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/session-repo-import/specs/session-management/spec.md

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 01:09:28)

Now I need to create the design.md. Let me read the design from the original change for context.

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/session-repo-import/design.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:09:43
**Parameters:**
content: ## Context

Session creation currently creates empty directories without repository files. Agents cannot bootstrap their workspace because:

1. No repository import happens during session creation
2. No Fossil HTTP server runs for agents to clone from
3. Tokens include sessionId/projectId but agents don't know where to work
4. Directory structure uses `worktree/` instead of `checkout/`/`upstream/`

The platform uses Fossil as an intermediary between Git/Fossil upstream repositories and agent workspaces. This design enables agents to clone, work, and sync changes uniformly regardless of the original VCS.

### Current State

- `projects/<id>/project.yaml`: Only stores metadata (repoUrl, repoType)
- `sessions/<id>/session.yaml`: Has assignedAgentId but no port
- `sessions/<id>/worktree/`: Empty directory
- `agents/<id>/agent.yaml`: Has single `sessionId` field
- `agents/service.ts`: Generates tokens with `{agentId, owner}` only
- Token you provided has `{agentId, sessionId, projectId, owner}` - generated elsewhere

### Constraints

- Fossil must be installed on platform server
- Port range 8000-9000 for Fossil HTTP servers
- Agent-token authentication via JWT
- One agent can have multiple sessions (1:many)
- Platform `checkout/` is source of truth for file sync

## Goals / Non-Goals

**Goals:**
- Session creation clones repo → imports to Fossil → opens checkout
- Fossil server starts on agent connect, stops on disconnect
- Agent fetches sessions via `GET /api/agents/me/sessions`
- Agent clones from `http://platform:port` to local workdir
- Platform applies agent changes to `checkout/`
- User commits from `checkout/` → exports to `upstream/` → pushes

**Non-Goals:**
- Bi-directional sync from upstream to Fossil proxy (one-time import only)
- Real-time file watching from platform
- Multi-user session collaboration

## Decisions

### 1. Session Directory Structure

**Decision:** Use three directories per session:

```
sessions/<session-id>/
├── session.yaml      # metadata + port
├── upstream/         # original repo (git clone or fossil clone)
├── repo.fossil       # fossil proxy (one-time import)
└── checkout/         # working copy (fossil open)
```

**Rationale:**
- `upstream/` preserves original repository for pushing
- `repo.fossil` isolates agent work from upstream
- `checkout/` is canonical for file sync and commits

**Alternative:** Single Fossil repo with push back to upstream
- **Rejected:** Requires bidirectional sync, more complex

### 2. Fossil Server Lifecycle

**Decision:** Start/stop per session on agent connect/disconnect.

```
Agent connects → fetch sessions → start fossil servers → send ports
Agent disconnects → stop fossil servers → release ports
```

**Rationale:**
- No server running = no resource waste when idle
- Agent-driven lifecycle = clear ownership
- Platform tracks port assignments in memory (could persist to session.yaml later)

**Alternative:** Start on session creation, stop on session delete
- **Rejected:** Wastes ports when session has no active agent

### 3. Token Design

**Decision:** Tokens contain only `{agentId, owner}`.

```typescript
const token = await new SignJWT({ 
  agentId: agent.id, 
  owner: agent.owner 
})
  .setProtectedHeader({ alg: "HS256" })
  .setIssuedAt()
  .setExpirationTime("24h")
  .sign(secret);
```

**Rationale:**
- One agent can have multiple sessions
- Session assignments change dynamically
- Agent fetches current sessions via API

**Alternative:** Token includes sessionIds array
- **Rejected:** Requires re-issuing token when sessions assigned/unassigned

### 4. Agent Session Discovery

**Decision:** REST API `GET /api/agents/me/sessions`.

```typescript
// Response
[
  {
    sessionId: "...",
    projectId: "...",
    sessionName: "fix-auth-bug",
    status: "active",
    port: 8042
  }
]
```

**Rationale:**
- Simple REST call on agent startup and after connect
- No state in token, all state in API
- Can add filtering/pagination later

**Alternative:** WebSocket message with session list
- **Rejected:** REST is simpler for one-time fetch; WebSocket for real-time updates

### 5. Commit Flow

**Decision:** Three-step commit: fossil commit → export to upstream → push to remote.

```
checkout/ (fossil) → repo.fossil → upstream/ → remote
```

```bash
# In checkout/
fossil commit -m "message"

# Export to upstream
cd ../upstream
fossil export --git ../repo.fossil | git apply

# Push
git push origin main
```

**Rationale:**
- Fossil tracks all changes in `repo.fossil`
- `upstream/` stays in sync for push to origin
- Conflicts detected during `fossil export`

**Alternative:** Direct git commit in upstream, sync to fossil
- **Rejected:** Loses fossil benefits (audit trail, simpler merge)

### 6. Port Management

**Decision:** In-memory port pool with collision detection.

```typescript
const PORT_RANGE = { start: 8000, end: 9000 };
const portsInUse = new Set<number>();

function assignPort(): number | null {
  for (let port = PORT_RANGE.start; port <= PORT_RANGE.end; port++) {
    if (!portsInUse.has(port)) {
      portsInUse.add(port);
      return port;
    }
  }
  return null; // Exhausted
}
```

**Rationale:**
- Simple implementation
- Restart-safe (ports released on process restart)
- 1000 sessions supported

**Alternative:** Persist ports in session.yaml
- **Rejected:** Complexity for little benefit; ports released on restart anyway

## Risks / Trade-offs

**[Risk]** Port exhaustion with many sessions
→ **Mitigation:** 1000 ports (8000-9000) is high limit; monitor usage; error clearly

**[Risk]** Fossil server crashes leave orphaned processes
→ **Mitigation:** Track PIDs, kill on disconnect, health checks

**[Risk]** Agent disconnect doesn't stop server
→ **Mitigation:** 30-second grace period, then force stop; log warnings

**[Risk]** Clone fails mid-session creation
→ **Mitigation:** Rollback: delete partial session directory, return error

**[Risk]** Git pushes conflict with upstream changes
→ **Mitigation:** User must pull/merge in `upstream/` before push; platform shows git error

**[Trade-off]** One-time import means `repo.fossil` diverges from upstream
→ User can't pull new upstream changes into session; each session is isolated

**[Trade-off]** No persistent port assignments
→ Sessions lose port on platform restart; agents must reconnect

## Open Questions

1. **Should `upstream/` be lazily cloned on first commit?**
   - Currently: clone on session creation (upfront cost)
   - Alternative: clone only when user commits
   - **Decision:** Upfront clone - simpler, predictable

2. **How to handle `upstream/` pushing for Fossil repos?**
   - Git: `git push origin main`
   - Fossil: `fossil push URL`
   - **Decision:** VCS service handles both cases

3. **Should session.yaml persist `port` field?**
   - Current: in-memory only
   - Alternative: persist for debugging/inspection
   - **Decision:** Persist for observability
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/session-repo-import/design.md

````

@@ -0,0 +1,224 @@
+## Context
+
+Session creation currently creates empty directories without repository files. Agents cannot bootstrap their workspace because:
+
+1. No repository import happens during session creation
+2. No Fossil HTTP server runs for agents to clone from
+3. Tokens include sessionId/projectId but agents don't know where to work
+4. Directory structure uses `worktree/` instead of `checkout/`/`upstream/`
+
+The platform uses Fossil as an intermediary between Git/Fossil upstream repositories and agent workspaces. This design enables agents to clone, work, and sync changes uniformly regardless of the original VCS.
+
+### Current State
+
+- `projects/<id>/project.yaml`: Only stores metadata (repoUrl, repoType)
+- `sessions/<id>/session.yaml`: Has assignedAgentId but no port
+- `sessions/<id>/worktree/`: Empty directory
+- `agents/<id>/agent.yaml`: Has single `sessionId` field
+- `agents/service.ts`: Generates tokens with `{agentId, owner}` only
+- Token you provided has `{agentId, sessionId, projectId, owner}` - generated elsewhere
+
+### Constraints
+
+- Fossil must be installed on platform server
+- Port range 8000-9000 for Fossil HTTP servers
+- Agent-token authentication via JWT
+- One agent can have multiple sessions (1:many)
+- Platform `checkout/` is source of truth for file sync
+
+## Goals / Non-Goals
+
+**Goals:**
+- Session creation clones repo → imports to Fossil → opens checkout
+- Fossil server starts on agent connect, stops on disconnect
+- Agent fetches sessions via `GET /api/agents/me/sessions`
+- Agent clones from `http://platform:port` to local workdir
+- Platform applies agent changes to `checkout/`
+- User commits from `checkout/` → exports to `upstream/` → pushes
+
+**Non-Goals:**
+- Bi-directional sync from upstream to Fossil proxy (one-time import only)
+- Real-time file watching from platform
+- Multi-user session collaboration
+
+## Decisions
+
+### 1. Session Directory Structure
+
+**Decision:** Use three directories per session:
+
+```
+sessions/<session-id>/
+├── session.yaml      # metadata + port
+├── upstream/         # original repo (git clone or fossil clone)
+├── repo.fossil       # fossil proxy (one-time import)
+└── checkout/         # working copy (fossil open)
+```
+
+**Rationale:**
+- `upstream/` preserves original repository for pushing
+- `repo.fossil` isolates agent work from upstream
+- `checkout/` is canonical for file sync and commits
+
+**Alternative:** Single Fossil repo with push back to upstream
+- **Rejected:** Requires bidirectional sync, more complex
+
+### 2. Fossil Server Lifecycle
+
+**Decision:** Start/stop per session on agent connect/disconnect.
+
+```
+Agent connects → fetch sessions → start fossil servers → send ports
+Agent disconnects → stop fossil servers → release ports
+```
+
+**Rationale:**
+- No server running = no resource waste when idle
+- Agent-driven lifecycle = clear ownership
+- Platform tracks port assignments in memory (could persist to session.yaml later)
+
+**Alternative:** Start on session creation, stop on session delete
+- **Rejected:** Wastes ports when session has no active agent
+
+### 3. Token Design
+
+**Decision:** Tokens contain only `{agentId, owner}`.
+
+```typescript
+const token = await new SignJWT({ 
+  agentId: agent.id, 
+  owner: agent.owner 
+})
+  .setProtectedHeader({ alg: "HS256" })
+  .setIssuedAt()
+  .setExpirationTime("24h")
+  .sign(secret);
+```
+
+**Rationale:**
+- One agent can have multiple sessions
+- Session assignments change dynamically
+- Agent fetches current sessions via API
+
+**Alternative:** Token includes sessionIds array
+- **Rejected:** Requires re-issuing token when sessions assigned/unassigned
+
+### 4. Agent Session Discovery
+
+**Decision:** REST API `GET /api/agents/me/sessions`.
+
+```typescript
+// Response
+[
+  {
+    sessionId: "...",
+    projectId: "...",
+    sessionName: "fix-auth-bug",
+    status: "active",
+    port: 8042
+  }
+]
+```
+
+**Rationale:**
+- Simple REST call on agent startup and after connect
+- No state in token, all state in API
+- Can add filtering/pagination later
+
+**Alternative:** WebSocket message with session list
+- **Rejected:** REST is simpler for one-time fetch; WebSocket for real-time updates
+
+### 5. Commit Flow
+
+**Decision:** Three-step commit: fossil commit → export to upstream → push to remote.
+
+```
+checkout/ (fossil) → repo.fossil → upstream/ → remote
+```
+
+```bash
+# In checkout/
+fossil commit -m "message"
+
+# Export to upstream
+cd ../upstream
+fossil export --git ../repo.fossil | git apply
+
+# Push
+git push origin main
+```
+
+**Rationale:**
+- Fossil tracks all changes in `repo.fossil`
+- `upstream/` stays in sync for push to origin
+- Conflicts detected during `fossil export`
+
+**Alternative:** Direct git commit in upstream, sync to fossil
+- **Rejected:** Loses fossil benefits (audit trail, simpler merge)
+
+### 6. Port Management
+
+**Decision:** In-memory port pool with collision detection.
+
+```typescript
+const PORT_RANGE = { start: 8000, end: 9000 };
+const portsInUse = new Set<number>();
+
+function assignPort(): number | null {
+  for (let port = PORT_RANGE.start; port <= PORT_RANGE.end; port++) {
+    if (!portsInUse.has(port)) {
+      portsInUse.add(port);
+      return port;
+    }
+  }
+  return null; // Exhausted
+}
+```
+
+**Rationale:**
+- Simple implementation
+- Restart-safe (ports released on process restart)
+- 1000 sessions supported
+
+**Alternative:** Persist ports in session.yaml
+- **Rejected:** Complexity for little benefit; ports released on restart anyway
+
+## Risks / Trade-offs
+
+**[Risk]** Port exhaustion with many sessions
+→ **Mitigation:** 1000 ports (8000-9000) is high limit; monitor usage; error clearly
+
+**[Risk]** Fossil server crashes leave orphaned processes
+→ **Mitigation:** Track PIDs, kill on disconnect, health checks
+
+**[Risk]** Agent disconnect doesn't stop server
+→ **Mitigation:** 30-second grace period, then force stop; log warnings
+
+**[Risk]** Clone fails mid-session creation
+→ **Mitigation:** Rollback: delete partial session directory, return error
+
+**[Risk]** Git pushes conflict with upstream changes
+→ **Mitigation:** User must pull/merge in `upstream/` before push; platform shows git error
+
+**[Trade-off]** One-time import means `repo.fossil` diverges from upstream
+→ User can't pull new upstream changes into session; each session is isolated
+
+**[Trade-off]** No persistent port assignments
+→ Sessions lose port on platform restart; agents must reconnect
+
+## Open Questions
+
+1. **Should `upstream/` be lazily cloned on first commit?**
+   - Currently: clone on session creation (upfront cost)
+   - Alternative: clone only when user commits
+   - **Decision:** Upfront clone - simpler, predictable
+
+2. **How to handle `upstream/` pushing for Fossil repos?**
+   - Git: `git push origin main`
+   - Fossil: `fossil push URL`
+   - **Decision:** VCS service handles both cases
+
+3. **Should session.yaml persist `port` field?**
+   - Current: in-memory only
+   - Alternative: persist for debugging/inspection
+   - **Decision:** Persist for observability

## Summary

**Change:** `session-repo-import`

| Artifact | Description |
|----------|-------------|
| `proposal.md` | Why this change is needed, what changes, impact |

| `specs/` | 6 specification files |
| `tasks.md` | 41 implementation tasks in 9 groups |

##### Key Design Decisions

1. **Session directories**: `upstream/` (original repo), `repo.fossil` (proxy), `checkout/` (working copy)
2. **Token**: Only `{agentId, owner}` - sessions fetched via API
3. **Fossil server**: Starts on agent connect, stops on disconnect, port 8000-9000
4. **Commit flow**: fossil commit → export to upstream → push to remote

### Ready for Implementation

Run `/opsx:apply` to start implementing.

4: import { dump, load } from "js-yaml";

33:   projectId: string;
34:   owner: string;
35:   worktreePath: string;

37: }

39: export class SessionRepository {
40:   private getSessionPath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
41:     return join(getPaths().projects, projectId, "sessions", sessionId);
42:   }
43: 
44:   private getSessionFilePath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
45:     return join(this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId), "session.yaml");
46:   }
47: 
48:   private generateId(): string {
49:     return crypto.randomUUID();
50:   }
51: 
52:   private getWorktreePath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
53:     return join(getPaths().projects, projectId, "worktrees", sessionId);
54:   }
55: 
56:   async create(input: CreateSessionInput): Promise<Session> {
57:     const id = this.generateId();
58:     const sessionPath = this.getSessionPath(input.projectId, id);
59:     const worktreePath = this.getWorktreePath(input.projectId, id);
60:     
61:     // Create session directory
62:     if (!existsSync(sessionPath)) {
63:       mkdirSync(sessionPath, { recursive: true });
64:     }
65: 
66:     // Create worktree directory
67:     if (!existsSync(worktreePath)) {
68:       mkdirSync(worktreePath, { recursive: true });
69:     }
70: 
71:     const now = new Date().toISOString();
72:     const sessionData: SessionData = {
73:       id,
74:       name: input.name,
75:       projectId: input.projectId,
76:       owner: input.owner,
77:       worktreePath,
78:       assignedAgentId: input.assignedAgentId,
79:       status: "active",
80:       createdAt: now,
81:       updatedAt: now,
82:     };
83: 
84:     writeFileSync(
85:       this.getSessionFilePath(input.projectId, id),
86:       dump(sessionData),
87:       "utf-8"
88:     );
89: 
90:     return {
91:       ...sessionData,
92:       createdAt: new Date(sessionData.createdAt),
93:       updatedAt: new Date(sessionData.updatedAt),
94:     };
95:   }
96: 
97:   async findById(sessionId: string): Promise<Session | null> {
98:     // Search across all projects for the session
99:     const Paths = getPaths();
100:     if (!existsSync(Paths.projects)) {
101:       return null;
102:     }
103: 
104:     const projectEntries = readdirSync(Paths.projects, { withFileTypes: true });
105:     
106:     for (const projectEntry of projectEntries) {
107:       if (projectEntry.isDirectory()) {
108:         const sessionsDir = join(Paths.projects, projectEntry.name, "sessions");
109:         if (existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
110:           const sessionFile = join(sessionsDir, sessionId, "session.yaml");
111:           if (existsSync(sessionFile)) {
112:             const content = readFileSync(sessionFile, "utf-8");
113:             const data = load(content) as SessionData;
114:             return {
115:               ...data,
116:               createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
117:               updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
118:             };
119:           }
120:         }
121:       }
122:     }
123: 
124:     return null;
125:   }
126: 
127:   async findByProjectAndId(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<Session | null> {
128:     const filePath = this.getSessionFilePath(projectId, sessionId);
129:     if (!existsSync(filePath)) {
130:       return null;
131:     }
132: 
133:     const content = readFileSync(filePath, "utf-8");
134:     const data = load(content) as SessionData;
135:     
136:     return {
137:       ...data,
138:       createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
139:       updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
140:     };
141:   }
142: 
143:   async listByProject(projectId: string): Promise<Session[]> {
144:     const sessionsDir = join(getPaths().projects, projectId, "sessions");
145:     if (!existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
146:       return [];
147:     }
148: 
149:     const entries = readdirSync(sessionsDir, { withFileTypes: true });
150:     const sessions: Session[] = [];
151: 
152:     for (const entry of entries) {
153:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
154:         const sessionFile = join(sessionsDir, entry.name, "session.yaml");
155:         if (existsSync(sessionFile)) {
156:           const content = readFileSync(sessionFile, "utf-8");
157:           const data = load(content) as SessionData;
158:           sessions.push({
159:             ...data,
160:             createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
161:             updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
162:           });
163:         }
164:       }
165:     }
166: 
167:     return sessions.sort((a, b) => b.createdAt.getTime() - a.createdAt.getTime());
168:   }
169: 
170:   async findByAssignedAgentId(agentId: string): Promise<Session[]> {
171:     const Paths = getPaths();
172:     if (!existsSync(Paths.projects)) {
173:       return [];
174:     }
175: 
176:     const projectEntries = readdirSync(Paths.projects, { withFileTypes: true });
177:     const sessions: Session[] = [];
178: 
179:     for (const projectEntry of projectEntries) {
180:       if (projectEntry.isDirectory()) {
181:         const sessionsDir = join(Paths.projects, projectEntry.name, "sessions");
182:         if (existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
183:           const entries = readdirSync(sessionsDir, { withFileTypes: true });
184:           for (const entry of entries) {
185:             if (entry.isDirectory()) {
186:               const sessionFile = join(sessionsDir, entry.name, "session.yaml");
187:               if (existsSync(sessionFile)) {
188:                 const content = readFileSync(sessionFile, "utf-8");
189:                 const data = load(content) as SessionData;
190:                 if (data.assignedAgentId === agentId) {
191:                   sessions.push({
192:                     ...data,
193:                     createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
194:                     updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
195:                   });
196:                 }
197:               }
198:             }
199:           }
200:         }
201:       }
202:     }
203: 
204:     return sessions.sort((a, b) => b.createdAt.getTime() - a.createdAt.getTime());
205:   }
206: 
207:   async update(sessionId: string, updates: Partial<Omit<SessionData, "id" | "createdAt">>): Promise<Session | null> {
208:     const session = await this.findById(sessionId);
209:     if (!session) return null;
210: 
211:     const updatedData: SessionData = {
212:       ...session,
213:       ...updates,
214:       updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
215:     };
216: 
217:     const filePath = this.getSessionFilePath(session.projectId, sessionId);
218:     writeFileSync(filePath, dump(updatedData), "utf-8");
219: 
220:     return {
221:       ...updatedData,
222:       createdAt: new Date(updatedData.createdAt),
223:       updatedAt: new Date(updatedData.updatedAt),
224:     };
225:   }
226: 
227:   async delete(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
228:     const sessionPath = this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId);
229:     
230:     // Get session to find worktree path
231:     const session = await this.findByProjectAndId(projectId, sessionId);
232:     
233:     if (session && existsSync(session.worktreePath)) {
234:       // Delete worktree directory
235:       this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(session.worktreePath);
236:     }
237:     
238:     // Delete session directory
239:     if (existsSync(sessionPath)) {
240:       this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(sessionPath);
241:     }
242:   }
243: 
244:   private deleteDirectoryRecursive(dirPath: string): void {
245:     if (!existsSync(dirPath)) return;
246: 
247:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
248:     
249:     for (const entry of entries) {
250:       const entryPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
251:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
252:         this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(entryPath);
253:       } else {
254:         unlinkSync(entryPath);
255:       }
256:     }
257: 
258:     rmdirSync(dirPath);
259:   }
260: 
261:   async exists(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<boolean> {
262:     return existsSync(this.getSessionFilePath(projectId, sessionId));
263:   }
264: }

filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/sessions/repository.ts
newString:   private getSessionPath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
    return join(getPaths().projects, projectId, "sessions", sessionId);
  }

  private getSessionFilePath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
    return join(this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId), "session.yaml");
  }

  private getUpstreamPath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
    return join(this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId), "upstream");
  }

  private getCheckoutPath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
    return join(this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId), "checkout");
  }

  private generateId(): string {
    return crypto.randomUUID();
  }

  async create(input: CreateSessionInput): Promise<Session> {
    const id = this.generateId();
    const sessionPath = this.getSessionPath(input.projectId, id);
    const upstreamPath = this.getUpstreamPath(input.projectId, id);
    const checkoutPath = this.getCheckoutPath(input.projectId, id);
    
    // Create session directory
    if (!existsSync(sessionPath)) {
      mkdirSync(sessionPath, { recursive: true });
    }

    // Create upstream directory
    if (!existsSync(upstreamPath)) {
      mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
    }

    // Create checkout directory
    if (!existsSync(checkoutPath)) {
      mkdirSync(checkoutPath, { recursive: true });
    }

    const now = new Date().toISOString();
    const sessionData: SessionData = {
      id,
      name: input.name,
      projectId: input.projectId,
      owner: input.owner,
      upstreamPath,
      checkoutPath,
      assignedAgentId: input.assignedAgentId,
      status: "active",
      createdAt: now,
      updatedAt: now,
    };

    writeFileSync(
      this.getSessionFilePath(input.projectId, id),
      dump(sessionData),
      "utf-8"
    );

    return {
      ...sessionData,
      createdAt: new Date(sessionData.createdAt),
      updatedAt: new Date(sessionData.updatedAt),
    };
  }
oldString:   private getSessionPath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {

    const worktreePath = this.getWorktreePath(input.projectId, id);

      this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(sessionPath);

oldString:   async delete(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
    const sessionPath = this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId);
    
    // Get session to find worktree path
    const session = await this.findByProjectAndId(projectId, sessionId);
    
    if (session && existsSync(session.worktreePath)) {
      // Delete worktree directory
      this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(session.worktreePath);
    }
    
    // Delete session directory
    if (existsSync(sessionPath)) {
      this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(sessionPath);
    }
  }

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 01:11:42)

Now I need to add methods for:
1. cloneRepository() - for Git and Fossil URL cloning
2. importToFossil() - for Git → Fossil and Fossil clone
3. openFossilCheckout() - to open checkout directory

Let me add these methods after the existing methods.

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/vcs/index.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:11:49
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/vcs/index.ts
newString:   async getCommitHistory(workDir: string, limit: number = 10): Promise<VCSResult> {
    const result = await this.execCommand(
      ["fossil", "timeline", "-n", limit.toString()],
      workDir
    );

    return {
      success: result.success,
      output: result.output,
      error: result.error || undefined,
    };
  }

  async cloneRepository(
    repoUrl: string,
    repoType: "git" | "fossil",
    targetDir: string
  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
    const { mkdirSync } = await import("fs");
    
    // Ensure target directory exists
    try {
      mkdirSync(targetDir, { recursive: true });
    } catch {
      // Directory might already exist
    }

    if (repoType === "git") {
      // Clone Git repository
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["git", "clone", repoUrl, targetDir],
        targetDir
      );
      
      if (result.success) {
        return {
          success: true,
          output: result.output,
        };
      }
      
      // If git clone failed but directory has content, try cloning into current directory
      const result2 = await this.execCommand(
        ["git", "clone", repoUrl, "."],
        targetDir
      );
      
      return {
        success: result2.success,
        output: result2.output,
        error: result2.error || undefined,
      };
    } else {
      // Clone Fossil repository
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["fossil", "clone", repoUrl, `${targetDir}/.fossil`],
        targetDir
      );
      
      if (result.success) {
        // Open the cloned repo in the target directory
        const openResult = await this.openFossil(
          `${targetDir}/.fossil`,
          targetDir
        );
        return openResult;
      }
      
      return {
        success: false,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || "Failed to clone Fossil repository",
      };
    }
  }

  async importToFossil(
    upstreamPath: string,
    repoType: "git" | "fossil",
    fossilPath: string
  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
    if (repoType === "git") {
      // Import from Git to Fossil
      // First create the fossil repo
      const initResult = await this.createFossilRepo(fossilPath);
      if (!initResult.success) {
        return initResult;
      }
      
      // Import from git bundle or directory
      const gitDir = `${upstreamPath}/.git`;
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["fossil", "import", "--git", gitDir, fossilPath],
        upstreamPath
      );
      
      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    } else {
      // For fossil, clone from the upstream fossil repo
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["fossil", "clone", `${upstreamPath}/.fossil`, fossilPath],
        upstreamPath
      );
      
      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    }
  }

  async openFossilCheckout(
    fossilPath: string,
    checkoutPath: string
  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
    const { mkdirSync } = await import("fs");
    
    // Ensure checkout directory exists
    try {
      mkdirSync(checkoutPath, { recursive: true });
    } catch {
      // Directory might already exist
    }
    
    // Open the fossil repo in the checkout directory
    const result = await this.execCommand(
      ["fossil", "open", fossilPath],
      checkoutPath
    );
    
    return {
      success: result.success,
      output: result.output,
      error: result.error || undefined,
    };
  }
oldString:   async getCommitHistory(workDir: string, limit: number = 10): Promise<VCSResult> {
    const result = await this.execCommand(
      ["fossil", "timeline", "-n", limit.toString()],
      workDir
    );

    return {
      success: result.success,
      output: result.output,
      error: result.error || undefined,
    };
  }

```

+      
+      // Import from git bundle or directory
+      const gitDir = `${upstreamPath}/.git`;
+      const result = await this.execCommand(
+        ["fossil", "import", "--git", gitDir, fossilPath],
+        upstreamPath
+      );
+      
+      return {
+        success: result.success,
+        output: result.output,
+        error: result.error || undefined,
+      };
+    } else {
+      // For fossil, clone from the upstream fossil repo
+      const result = await this.execCommand(
+        ["fossil", "clone", `${upstreamPath}/.fossil`, fossilPath],
+        upstreamPath
+      );
+      
+      return {
+        success: result.success,
+        output: result.output,
+        error: result.error || undefined,
+      };
+    }
+  }
+
+  async openFossilCheckout(
+    fossilPath: string,
+    checkoutPath: string
+  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
+    const { mkdirSync } = await import("fs");
+    
+    // Ensure checkout directory exists
+    try {
+      mkdirSync(checkoutPath, { recursive: true });
+    } catch {
+      // Directory might already exist
+    }
+    
+    // Open the fossil repo in the checkout directory
+    const result = await this.execCommand(
+      ["fossil", "open", fossilPath],
+      checkoutPath
+    );
+    
+    return {
+      success: result.success,
+      output: result.output,
+      error: result.error || undefined,
+    };
   }
\ No newline at end of file
```

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/sessions/routes.tsx

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:12:36
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/sessions/routes.tsx
newString: // POST /sessions or /projects/:projectId/sessions - Create new session
router.post("/", async (c: Context) => {
  const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
  if (!username) {
    return c.redirect("/auth/login");
  }

  const body = await c.req.parseBody();
  const name = body.name as string;
  const projectId = (body.projectId as string) || getProjectId(c);
  const assignedAgentId = (body.assignedAgentId as string) || null;

  if (!name || !projectId) {
    return c.text("Name and project ID required", 400);
  }

  const project = await projectRepository.findById(projectId);
  if (!project || project.owner !== username) {
    return c.text("Project not found", 404);
  }

  // Create session with upstream and checkout directories
  const session = await sessionRepository.create({
    name: name as string,
    projectId: projectId as string,
    owner: username,
    assignedAgentId: assignedAgentId || undefined,
  });

  // Initialize repository: clone → import to fossil → open checkout
  try {
    // Step 1: Clone repository to upstream/
    const cloneResult = await vcs.cloneRepository(
      project.repoUrl,
      project.repoType,
      session.upstreamPath
    );
    
    if (!cloneResult.success) {
      await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
      return c.text(`Failed to clone repository: ${cloneResult.error}`, 500);
    }

    // Step 2: Import to fossil proxy (repo.fossil)
    const fossilPath = `${session.upstreamPath}/../repo.fossil`;
    const importResult = await vcs.importToFossil(
      session.upstreamPath,
      project.repoType,
      fossilPath
    );
    
    if (!importResult.success) {
      await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
      return c.text(`Failed to import to fossil: ${importResult.error}`, 500);
    }

    // Step 3: Open fossil checkout
    const checkoutResult = await vcs.openFossilCheckout(
      fossilPath,
      session.checkoutPath
    );
    
    if (!checkoutResult.success) {
      await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
      return c.text(`Failed to open checkout: ${checkoutResult.error}`, 500);
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Failed to setup session:", error);
    await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
    return c.text("Failed to setup session repository", 500);
  }

  return c.redirect(`/projects/${projectId}/sessions/${session.id}`);
});
oldString: // POST /sessions or /projects/:projectId/sessions - Create new session
router.post("/", async (c: Context) => {
  const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
  if (!username) {
    return c.redirect("/auth/login");
  }

  const body = await c.req.parseBody();
  const name = body.name as string;
  const projectId = (body.projectId as string) || getProjectId(c);
  const assignedAgentId = (body.assignedAgentId as string) || null;

  if (!name || !projectId) {
    return c.text("Name and project ID required", 400);
  }

  const project = await projectRepository.findById(projectId);
  if (!project || project.owner !== username) {
    return c.text("Project not found", 404);
  }

  // Create session with worktree
  const session = await sessionRepository.create({
    name: name as string,
    projectId: projectId as string,
    owner: username,
    worktreePath: "", // Will be set by repository
    assignedAgentId: assignedAgentId || undefined,
  });

  // Initialize worktree from Fossil repository
  try {
    await vcs.setupSessionWorktree(projectId, session.id, session.worktreePath);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Failed to setup worktree:", error);
    // Don't fail - user can still see the session
  }

  return c.redirect(`/projects/${projectId}/sessions/${session.id}`);
});

51:       return {
52:         agentId: payload.agentId as string,
53:         owner: payload.owner as string,
54:       };
55:     } catch {
56:       return null;
57:     }
58:   }

62:     if (!agent) {
63:       ws.close(1008, "Agent not found");
64:       return;
65:     }
66: 
67:     this.activeConnections.set(agentId, ws);
68:     await this.repository.updateStatus(agentId, "online");
69:     await this.repository.updateLastActivity(agentId);
70:   }
71:

73:     this.activeConnections.delete(agentId);

80:     if (!session || !session.assignedAgentId) {
81:       return false;
82:     }

86:       return false;

110:       this.activeConnections.delete(agentId);
111:     }

17:   updatedAt: Date;
18:   lastActivityAt?: Date;
19: }

22:   id: string;
23:   owner: string;
24:   token: string;
25:   status: AgentStatus;
26:   startedAt: string;
27:   updatedAt: string;
28:   lastActivityAt?: string;
29: }
30: 
31: export interface CreateAgentInput {
32:   owner: string;
33: }
34: 
35: export class AgentRepository {
36:   private getAgentPath(agentId: string): string {
37:     return join(getPaths().agents, agentId);
38:   }
39: 
40:   private getAgentFilePath(agentId: string): string {
41:     return join(this.getAgentPath(agentId), "agent.yaml");
42:   }
43: 
44:   private generateId(): string {
45:     return crypto.randomUUID();
46:   }
47: 
48:   async create(input: CreateAgentInput): Promise<Agent> {
49:     const id = this.generateId();
50:     const agentPath = this.getAgentPath(id);
51:     
52:     if (!existsSync(agentPath)) {
53:       mkdirSync(agentPath, { recursive: true });
54:     }
55: 
56:     const now = new Date().toISOString();
57:     const agentData: AgentData = {
58:       id,
59:       owner: input.owner,
60:       token: crypto.randomUUID(), // Temporary placeholder, service will update with JWT
61:       status: "offline",
62:       startedAt: now,
63:       updatedAt: now,
64:     };
65: 
66:     writeFileSync(this.getAgentFilePath(id), dump(agentData), "utf-8");
67: 
68:     return {
69:       ...agentData,
70:       startedAt: new Date(agentData.startedAt),
71:       updatedAt: new Date(agentData.updatedAt),
72:       lastActivityAt: agentData.lastActivityAt 
73:         ? new Date(agentData.lastActivityAt) 
74:         : undefined,
75:     };
76:   }
77: 
78:   async findById(agentId: string): Promise<Agent | null> {
79:     const filePath = this.getAgentFilePath(agentId);
80:     if (!existsSync(filePath)) {
81:       return null;
82:     }
83: 
84:     const content = readFileSync(filePath, "utf-8");
85:     const data = load(content) as AgentData;
86: 
87:     return {
88:       ...data,
89:       startedAt: new Date(data.startedAt),
90:       updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
91:       lastActivityAt: data.lastActivityAt 
92:         ? new Date(data.lastActivityAt) 
93:         : undefined,
94:     };
95:   }
96: 
97:   async findByStatus(status: AgentStatus): Promise<Agent[]> {
98:     const Paths = getPaths();
99:     if (!existsSync(Paths.agents)) {
100:       return [];
101:     }
102: 
103:     const entries = readdirSync(Paths.agents, { withFileTypes: true });
104:     const agents: Agent[] = [];
105: 
106:     for (const entry of entries) {
107:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
108:         const agentFile = join(Paths.agents, entry.name, "agent.yaml");
109:         if (existsSync(agentFile)) {
110:           const content = readFileSync(agentFile, "utf-8");
111:           const data = load(content) as AgentData;
112:           if (data.status === status) {
113:             agents.push({
114:               ...data,
115:               startedAt: new Date(data.startedAt),
116:               updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
117:               lastActivityAt: data.lastActivityAt 
118:                 ? new Date(data.lastActivityAt) 
119:                 : undefined,
120:             });
121:           }
122:         }
123:       }
124:     }
125: 
126:     return agents.sort((a, b) => b.startedAt.getTime() - a.startedAt.getTime());
127:   }
128: 
129:   async findByOwner(owner: string): Promise<Agent[]> {
130:     const Paths = getPaths();
131:     if (!existsSync(Paths.agents)) {
132:       return [];
133:     }
134: 
135:     const entries = readdirSync(Paths.agents, { withFileTypes: true });
136:     const agents: Agent[] = [];
137: 
138:     for (const entry of entries) {
139:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
140:         const agentFile = join(Paths.agents, entry.name, "agent.yaml");
141:         if (existsSync(agentFile)) {
142:           const content = readFileSync(agentFile, "utf-8");
143:           const data = load(content) as AgentData;
144:           if (data.owner === owner) {
145:             agents.push({
146:               ...data,
147:               startedAt: new Date(data.startedAt),
148:               updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
149:               lastActivityAt: data.lastActivityAt 
150:                 ? new Date(data.lastActivityAt) 
151:                 : undefined,
152:             });
153:           }
154:         }
155:       }
156:     }
157: 
158:     return agents.sort((a, b) => b.startedAt.getTime() - a.startedAt.getTime());
159:   }
160: 
161:   async update(
162:     agentId: string, 
163:     updates: Partial<Omit<AgentData, "id" | "startedAt">>
164:   ): Promise<Agent | null> {
165:     const agent = await this.findById(agentId);
166:     if (!agent) return null;
167: 
168:     const updatedData: AgentData = {
169:       ...agent,
170:       ...updates,
171:       updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
172:     };
173: 
174:     const filePath = this.getAgentFilePath(agentId);
175:     writeFileSync(filePath, dump(updatedData), "utf-8");
176: 
177:     return {
178:       ...updatedData,
179:       startedAt: new Date(updatedData.startedAt),
180:       updatedAt: new Date(updatedData.updatedAt),
181:       lastActivityAt: updatedData.lastActivityAt 
182:         ? new Date(updatedData.lastActivityAt) 
183:         : undefined,
184:     };
185:   }
186: 
187:   async updateStatus(agentId: string, status: AgentStatus): Promise<Agent | null> {
188:     return this.update(agentId, { status });
189:   }
190: 
191:   async updateLastActivity(agentId: string): Promise<Agent | null> {
192:     return this.update(agentId, { lastActivityAt: new Date().toISOString() });
193:   }
194: 
195:   async delete(agentId: string): Promise<void> {
196:     const agentPath = this.getAgentPath(agentId);
197:     if (existsSync(agentPath)) {
198:       this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(agentPath);
199:     }
200:   }
201: 
202:   private deleteDirectoryRecursive(dirPath: string): void {
203:     if (!existsSync(dirPath)) return;
204: 
205:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
206:     
207:     for (const entry of entries) {
208:       const entryPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
209:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
210:         this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(entryPath);
211:       } else {
212:         unlinkSync(entryPath);
213:       }
214:     }
215: 
216:     rmdirSync(dirPath);
217:   }
218: 
219:   async exists(agentId: string): Promise<boolean> {
220:     return existsSync(this.getAgentFilePath(agentId));
221:   }
222: }

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/agents/repository.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:14:04
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/agents/repository.ts
newString:   async updateLastActivity(agentId: string): Promise<Agent | null> {
    return this.update(agentId, { lastActivityAt: new Date().toISOString() });
  }

  async assignSession(agentId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<Agent | null> {
    const agent = await this.findById(agentId);
    if (!agent) return null;
    
    if (!agent.sessionIds.includes(sessionId)) {
      const updatedSessionIds = [...agent.sessionIds, sessionId];
      return this.update(agentId, { sessionIds: updatedSessionIds });
    }
    return agent;
  }

  async unassignSession(agentId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<Agent | null> {
    const agent = await this.findById(agentId);
    if (!agent) return null;
    
    const updatedSessionIds = agent.sessionIds.filter(id => id !== sessionId);
    return this.update(agentId, { sessionIds: updatedSessionIds });
  }

  async delete(agentId: string): Promise<void> {

  }
