## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 01:14:29)

I need to add a new API endpoint that doesn't require auth middleware - it should use the agent JWT token. Let me create a new route for this.

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/agents/routes.tsx

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:14:35
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/agents/routes.tsx
newString: /** @jsx jsx */
import { jsx } from "hono/jsx";
import { Hono } from "hono";
import { agentService, AgentTokenPayload } from "./service.js";
import { agentRepository } from "./repository.js";
import { sessionRepository } from "../sessions/repository.js";
import { Layout } from "../components/Layout.js";
import { authMiddleware } from "../auth/middleware.js";
import type { Context } from "hono";

const router = new Hono();

// Agent API endpoint - uses agent JWT, not user auth
router.get("/me/sessions", async (c: Context) => {
  const authHeader = c.req.header("Authorization");
  if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith("Bearer ")) {
    return c.json({ error: "Missing token" }, 401);
  }

  const token = authHeader.slice(7); // Remove "Bearer "
  const payload = await agentService.verifyAgentToken(token);
  if (!payload) {
    return c.json({ error: "Invalid token" }, 401);
  }

  const agent = await agentRepository.findById(payload.agentId);
  if (!agent) {
    return c.json({ error: "Agent not found" }, 404);
  }

  // Get all sessions assigned to this agent
  const sessions = await sessionRepository.findByAssignedAgentId(agent.id);
  
  return c.json(sessions.map(session => ({
    sessionId: session.id,
    projectId: session.projectId,
    sessionName: session.name,
    status: session.status,
    port: session.port,
  })));
});

router.use("/*", authMiddleware);
oldString: /** @jsx jsx */
import { jsx } from "hono/jsx";
import { Hono } from "hono";
import { agentService } from "./service.js";
import { agentRepository } from "./repository.js";
import { sessionRepository } from "../sessions/repository.js";
import { Layout } from "../components/Layout.js";
import { authMiddleware } from "../auth/middleware.js";
import type { Context } from "hono";

const router = new Hono();

router.use("/*", authMiddleware);

#### Task 4: Fossil Server Management

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/vcs/fossil-server.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:15:00
**Parameters:**
content: import { spawn, ChildProcess } from "child_process";
import { existsSync } from "fs";

const PORT_RANGE_START = 8000;
const PORT_RANGE_END = 9000;

interface RunningServer {
  port: number;
  process: ChildProcess;
  repoPath: string;
}

export class FossilServerManager {
  private portsInUse: Set<number> = new Set();
  private runningServers: Map<string, RunningServer> = new Map();

  assignPort(): number | null {
    for (let port = PORT_RANGE_START; port <= PORT_RANGE_END; port++) {
      if (!this.portsInUse.has(port)) {
        this.portsInUse.add(port);
        return port;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  releasePort(port: number): void {
    this.portsInUse.delete(port);
  }

  async startServer(sessionId: string, repoPath: string): Promise<{ port: number } | { error: string }> {
    // Check if server already running for this session
    if (this.runningServers.has(sessionId)) {
      const server = this.runningServers.get(sessionId)!;
      return { port: server.port };
    }

    // Check if repo exists
    if (!existsSync(repoPath)) {
      return { error: `Repository not found: ${repoPath}` };
    }

    // Assign port
    const port = this.assignPort();
    if (port === null) {
      return { error: "PORTS_EXHAUSTED" };
    }

    // Start fossil server
    const proc = spawn("fossil", ["server", "--port", port.toString(), repoPath], {
      stdio: "pipe",
      detached: false,
    });

    // Wait for server to start (simple check: wait a bit)
    await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 500));

    // Check if process started successfully
    if (proc.pid === undefined) {
      this.releasePort(port);
      return { error: "Failed to start Fossil server" };
    }

    // Track running server
    this.runningServers.set(sessionId, {
      port,
      process: proc,
      repoPath,
    });

    // Handle process exit
    proc.on("exit", () => {
      this.runningServers.delete(sessionId);
      this.releasePort(port);
    });

    return { port };
  }

  async stopServer(sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
    const server = this.runningServers.get(sessionId);
    if (!server) {
      return;
    }

    // Kill the process
    server.process.kill("SIGTERM");

    // Wait for process to exit
    await new Promise<void>((resolve) => {
      server.process.on("exit", () => {
        resolve();
      });
      // Force kill after 5 seconds
      setTimeout(() => {
        server.process.kill("SIGKILL");
        resolve();
      }, 5000);
    });

    // Cleanup
    this.runningServers.delete(sessionId);
    this.releasePort(server.port);
  }

  getRunningServer(sessionId: string): { port: number; repoPath: string } | null {
    const server = this.runningServers.get(sessionId);
    if (!server) {
      return null;
    }
    return { port: server.port, repoPath: server.repoPath };
  }

  isServerRunning(sessionId: string): boolean {
    return this.runningServers.has(sessionId);
  }

  getActiveServerCount(): number {
    return this.runningServers.size;
  }

  async stopAllServers(): Promise<void> {
    const stopPromises = Array.from(this.runningServers.keys()).map((sessionId) =>
      this.stopServer(sessionId)
    );
    await Promise.all(stopPromises);
  }
}

export const fossilServerManager = new FossilServerManager();

Now I need to update the close handler to stop Fossil servers when disconnecting. The current close handler just calls `agentService.handleAgentDisconnect`. I need to add a 30-second grace period before stopping servers on unexpected disconnect.

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/index.tsx

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:16:13
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/index.tsx
newString:     async close(ws) {
      const connectionType = ws.data?.connectionType;
      
      if (connectionType === 'chat') {
        // Remove from session subscribers
        const sessionId = ws.data.sessionId;
        if (chatSessions.has(sessionId)) {
          chatSessions.get(sessionId).delete(ws);
          if (chatSessions.get(sessionId).size === 0) {
            chatSessions.delete(sessionId);
          }
        }
        console.log(`Chat client disconnected from session ${sessionId}`);
      } else if (connectionType === 'agent') {
        const agentId = ws.data.agentId;
        if (agentId) {
          await agentService.handleAgentDisconnect(agentId);
          console.log(`Agent ${agentId} disconnected`);

          // Stop Fossil servers for assigned sessions after grace period
          const agent = await agentRepository.findById(agentId);
          if (agent && agent.sessionIds && agent.sessionIds.length > 0) {
            // 30-second grace period for unexpected disconnects
            setTimeout(async () => {
              // Check if agent reconnected
              if (!agentService.isAgentOnline(agentId)) {
                // Agent didn't reconnect, stop all servers
                for (const sessionId of agent.sessionIds) {
                  if (fossilServerManager.isServerRunning(sessionId)) {
                    await fossilServerManager.stopServer(sessionId);
                    console.log(`Stopped Fossil server for session ${sessionId}`);
                  }
                }
              }
            }, 30000);
          }
        }
      }
    },
oldString:     async close(ws) {

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/sync/service.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:16:58
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/sync/service.ts
newString: export interface FileSyncState {
  sessionId: string;
  upstreamPath: string;
  checkoutPath: string;
  changes: Map<string, FileChange>;
  baselineChecksums: Map<string, string>; // Track original checksums at last sync
  lastSyncAt?: Date;
}

export class FileSyncService {
  private syncStates: Map<string, FileSyncState> = new Map();
  private pendingChanges: Map<string, FileChange[]> = new Map(); // Buffered changes for reconnects

  async initializeSession(
    sessionId: string,
    checkoutPath: string,
    upstreamPath?: string
  ): Promise<void> {
    // Get paths from session if not provided
    if (!upstreamPath || !checkoutPath) {
      const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
      if (!session) {
        throw new Error(`Session ${sessionId} not found`);
      }
      
      upstreamPath = upstreamPath || session.upstreamPath;
      checkoutPath = checkoutPath || session.checkoutPath;
    }

    const syncState: FileSyncState = {
      sessionId,
      upstreamPath,
      checkoutPath,
      changes: new Map(),
      baselineChecksums: new Map(),
    };

    this.syncStates.set(sessionId, syncState);
    
    // Initialize empty pending changes buffer
    this.pendingChanges.set(sessionId, []);

    // Scan current state
    await this.scanSessionCheckout(sessionId);
  }
oldString: export interface FileSyncState {
  sessionId: string;
  originalRepoPath: string;
  sessionWorktreePath: string;
  changes: Map<string, FileChange>;
  baselineChecksums: Map<string, string>; // Track original checksums at last sync
  lastSyncAt?: Date;
}

export class FileSyncService {
  private syncStates: Map<string, FileSyncState> = new Map();
  private pendingChanges: Map<string, FileChange[]> = new Map(); // Buffered changes for reconnects

  async initializeSession(
    sessionId: string,
    sessionWorktreePath: string,
    originalRepoPath?: string
  ): Promise<void> {
    // Get original repo path from session if not provided
    if (!originalRepoPath) {
      const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
      if (!session) {
        throw new Error(`Session ${sessionId} not found`);
      }
      
      // Original repo is stored in the project's worktrees directory
      const { getProjectPath } = await import("../config/paths.js");
      const projectPath = getProjectPath(session.projectId);
      originalRepoPath = join(projectPath, "original");
    }

    const syncState: FileSyncState = {
      sessionId,
      originalRepoPath,
      sessionWorktreePath,
      changes: new Map(),
      baselineChecksums: new Map(),
    };

    this.syncStates.set(sessionId, syncState);
    
    // Initialize empty pending changes buffer
    this.pendingChanges.set(sessionId, []);

    // Scan current state
    await this.scanSessionWorktree(sessionId);
  }

118:       syncState!.changes.set(change.path, fileChange);
119:       fileChanges.push(fileChange);
120:     }
121: 
122:     // Sync changes to original repo
123:     await this.syncChangesToOriginal(sessionId, fileChanges);
124: 
125:     return fileChanges;
126:   }
127: 
128:   private async checkConflict(
129:     sessionId: string,
130:     filePath: string,
131:     agentStatus: FileStatus
132:   ): Promise<FileStatus | null> {
133:     const syncState = this.syncStates.get(sessionId);
134:     if (!syncState) return null;
135: 
136:     // Skip conflict check for new files
137:     if (agentStatus === "new") return null;
138: 
139:     const originalPath = join(syncState.originalRepoPath, filePath);
140:     
141:     // If file doesn't exist in original, no conflict
142:     if (!existsSync(originalPath)) {
143:       return null;
144:     }
145: 
146:     // Get checksums
147:     const sessionPath = join(syncState.sessionWorktreePath, filePath);
148:     
149:     if (!existsSync(sessionPath)) {
150:       // File was deleted in session but exists in original
151:       // Check if original was modified since last sync
152:       const originalChecksum = await this.calculateChecksum(originalPath);
153:       const baselineChecksum = syncState.baselineChecksums.get(filePath);
154:       
155:       if (baselineChecksum && originalChecksum !== baselineChecksum) {
156:         return "conflict";
157:       }
158:       return null;
159:     }
160: 
161:     // Compare checksums
162:     const originalChecksum = await this.calculateChecksum(originalPath);
163:     const sessionChecksum = await this.calculateChecksum(sessionPath);
164:     const baselineChecksum = syncState.baselineChecksums.get(filePath);
165: 
166:     // If original changed since last sync and agent also changed it, it's a conflict
167:     if (baselineChecksum && 
168:         originalChecksum !== baselineChecksum && 
169:         sessionChecksum !== baselineChecksum) {
170:       return "conflict";
171:     }
172: 
173:     return null;
174:   }

(Showing lines 75-174 of 489. Use offset=175 to continue.)
</content>
```

251:   async importToFossil(
252:     upstreamPath: string,
253:     repoType: "git" | "fossil",
254:     fossilPath: string
255:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
256:     if (repoType === "git") {
257:       // Import from Git to Fossil
258:       // First create the fossil repo
259:       const initResult = await this.createFossilRepo(fossilPath);
260:       if (!initResult.success) {
261:         return initResult;
262:       }
263:       
264:       // Import from git bundle or directory
265:       const gitDir = `${upstreamPath}/.git`;
266:       const result = await this.execCommand(
267:         ["fossil", "import", "--git", gitDir, fossilPath],
268:         upstreamPath
269:       );
270:       
271:       return {
272:         success: result.success,
273:         output: result.output,
274:         error: result.error || undefined,
275:       };

277:       // For fossil, clone from the upstream fossil repo
278:       const result = await this.execCommand(
279:         ["fossil", "clone", `${upstreamPath}/.fossil`, fossilPath],
280:         upstreamPath
281:       );
282:

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 01:18:58)

I need to add the exportFromFossil method to the VCS class. Let me add it after the openFossilCheckout method.

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/vcs/index.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:19:06
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/vcs/index.ts
newString:   async openFossilCheckout(
    fossilPath: string,
    checkoutPath: string
  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
    const { mkdirSync } = await import("fs");
    
    // Ensure checkout directory exists
    try {
      mkdirSync(checkoutPath, { recursive: true });
    } catch {
      // Directory might already exist
    }
    
    // Open the fossil repo in the checkout directory
    const result = await this.execCommand(
      ["fossil", "open", fossilPath],
      checkoutPath
    );
    
    return {
      success: result.success,
      output: result.output,
      error: result.error || undefined,
    };
  }

  async exportFromFossil(
    fossilPath: string,
    upstreamPath: string,
    repoType: "git" | "fossil"
  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
    if (repoType === "git") {
      // Export from Fossil to Git upstream
      // Use fossil export to create a git-fast-export stream
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["fossil", "export", "--git", fossilPath],
        upstreamPath
      );
      
      if (result.success) {
        // Apply the export to git
        const applyResult = await this.execCommand(
          ["git", "fast-import"],
          upstreamPath
        );
        return {
          success: applyResult.success,
          output: applyResult.output,
          error: applyResult.error || undefined,
        };
      }
      
      return {
        success: false,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    } else {
      // For fossil, push directly from checkout
      return {
        success: true,
        output: "Fossil repos sync directly",
      };
    }
  }

  async pushToRemote(
    upstreamPath: string,
    repoType: "git" | "fossil",
    remoteUrl?: string
  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
    if (repoType === "git") {
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["git", "push", "origin"],
        upstreamPath
      );
      
      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    } else {
      // Fossil push
      const args = remoteUrl ? ["push", remoteUrl] : ["push"];
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["fossil", ...args],
        upstreamPath
      );
      
      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    }
  }
oldString:   async openFossilCheckout(
    fossilPath: string,
    checkoutPath: string
  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
    const { mkdirSync } = await import("fs");
    
    // Ensure checkout directory exists
    try {
      mkdirSync(checkoutPath, { recursive: true });
    } catch {
      // Directory might already exist
    }
    
    // Open the fossil repo in the checkout directory
    const result = await this.execCommand(
      ["fossil", "open", fossilPath],
      checkoutPath
    );
    
    return {
      success: result.success,
      output: result.output,
      error: result.error || undefined,
    };
  }

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/session-repo-import/design.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:21:08
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/session-repo-import/design.md
limit: 50
offset: 55

````
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/session-repo-import/design.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>55: └── checkout/         # working copy (fossil open)
56: ```
57: 
58: **Rationale:**
59: - `upstream/` preserves original repository for pushing
60: - `repo.fossil` isolates agent work from upstream
61: - `checkout/` is canonical for file sync and commits
62: 
63: **Alternative:** Single Fossil repo with push back to upstream
64: - **Rejected:** Requires bidirectional sync, more complex
65: 
66: ### 2. Fossil Server Lifecycle
67: 
68: **Decision:** Start/stop per session on agent connect/disconnect.
69: 
70: ```
71: Agent connects → fetch sessions → start fossil servers → send ports
72: Agent disconnects → stop fossil servers → release ports
73: ```
74: 
75: **Rationale:**
76: - No server running = no resource waste when idle
77: - Agent-driven lifecycle = clear ownership
78: - Platform tracks port assignments in memory (could persist to session.yaml later)
79: 
80: **Alternative:** Start on session creation, stop on session delete
81: - **Rejected:** Wastes ports when session has no active agent
82: 
83: ### 3. Token Design
84: 
85: **Decision:** Tokens contain only `{agentId, owner}`.
86: 
87: ```typescript
88: const token = await new SignJWT({ 
89:   agentId: agent.id, 
90:   owner: agent.owner 
91: })
92:   .setProtectedHeader({ alg: "HS256" })
93:   .setIssuedAt()
94:   .setExpirationTime("24h")
95:   .sign(secret);
96: ```
97: 
98: **Rationale:**
99: - One agent can have multiple sessions
100: - Session assignments change dynamically
101: - Agent fetches current sessions via API
102: 
103: **Alternative:** Token includes sessionIds array
104: - **Rejected:** Requires re-issuing token when sessions assigned/unassigned

(Showing lines 55-104 of 224. Use offset=105 to continue.)
</content>
````

3: ### Requirement: Platform starts Fossil HTTP server when agent connects
4: 
5: The platform SHALL start a Fossil HTTP server for each session assigned to the connecting agent. 
6: 
7: #### Scenario: Agent connects with assigned sessions
8: - **WHEN** agent sends WebSocket message `agent_ready` with valid token
9: - **THEN** platform starts Fossil HTTP server for each assigned session
10: - **AND** platform assigns an available port from range 8000-9000

13: 
14: #### Scenario: No assigned sessions
15: - **WHEN** agent connects with no assigned sessions
16: - **THEN** platform sends empty `session_ready` array
17: - **AND** no Fossil servers are started
18: 
19: ### Requirement: Platform assigns unique ports for Fossil servers
20: 
21: The platform SHALL assign ports from range 8000-9000 with collision detection.
22: 
23: #### Scenario: Port assignment with available ports
24: - **WHEN** platform needs to start Fossil server
25: - **THEN** platform finds first available port in range 8000-9000
26: - **AND** platform marks port as in-use
27: - **AND** platform starts Fossil server on assigned port
28: 
29: #### Scenario: Port exhaustion
30: - **WHEN** all ports 8000-9000 are in use
31: - **THEN** platform returns error `PORTS_EXHAUSTED`
32: - **AND** session is marked as `error` state
33: 
34: ### Requirement: Platform stops Fossil server when agent disconnects
35: 
36: The platform SHALL stop Fossil HTTP servers for all sessions assigned to the disconnecting agent.
37: 
38: #### Scenario: Agent disconnects gracefully
39: - **WHEN** agent WebSocket closes normally
40: - **THEN** platform stops Fossil servers for all assigned sessions
41: - **AND** platform releases assigned ports
42: - **AND** platform marks sessions as `paused`
43: 
44: #### Scenario: Agent connection lost
45: - **WHEN** agent WebSocket closes unexpectedly or times out
46: - **THEN** platform stops Fossil servers after 30-second grace period
47: - **AND** platform releases assigned ports
48: - **AND** platform marks sessions as `paused`
49: 
50: ### Requirement: Fossil server serves repository for agent clone
51: 
52: The Fossil server SHALL serve the session's `repo.fossil` for agent cloning.
53: 
54: #### Scenario: Agent clones from Fossil server
55: - **WHEN** agent sends `fossil clone http://platform:port` request
56: - **THEN** Fossil server responds with repository data
57: - **AND** agent receives complete repository clone

## Verification Report: session-repo-import

##### Summary Scorecard

| Dimension    | Status                      |
|--------------|----------------------------|
| Completeness | 33/33 tasks complete       |
| Correctness  | All key requirements found |
| Coherence    | Design decisions followed  |

---

### ✅ CRITICAL Issues: None Found

---

### ⚠️ WARNINGS: 2

**WARNING 1: WebSocket handler may not start servers for unassignedAgents**

- **Location:** `src/index.tsx:223-239`
- **Issue:** The WebSocket handler iterates over `agent.sessionIds` to start Fossil servers, but sessions are assigned to agents via `assignedAgentId`. The relationship needs to be bidirectional.
- **Context:** Fossil servers start based on `agent.sessionIds` array, but sessions have `assignedAgentId`. When a session is assigned to an agent, the agent's `sessionIds` must be updated, and vice versa.
- **Recommendation:** Verify that when `assignedAgentId` is set on a session (via session creation or reassignment), the corresponding agent's `sessionIds` array is updated. Check `sessions/routes.tsx` POST handler to ensure `agentRepository.assignSession()` is called when `assignedAgentId` is provided.

**WARNING 2: Session port not persisted after Fossil server starts**

- **Location:** `src/index.tsx:231`, `fossil-server.ts`
- **Issue:** `sessionRepository.update(sessionId, { port: result.port })` is called, but the Session interface includes `port?: number`. Verify the update method supports this field.
- **Context:** The WS handler calls `sessionRepository.update(sessionId, { port: result.port })` but I should verify the update method signature accepts `port`.
- **Recommendation:** Check `sessions/repository.ts:update()` signature includes `port` in `Partial<Omit<SessionData, "id" | "createdAt">>`. If not, add it.

---

### 💡 SUGGESTIONS: 3

**SUGGESTION 1: Old `setupSessionWorktree` function still exists**

- **Location:** `vcs/index.ts:387-416`
- **Issue:** The old `setupSessionWorktree` function still references `worktreePath` and the old architecture pattern. It's no longer used by the session creation flow.
- **Recommendation:** Consider removing or deprecating this function since session creation now uses `cloneRepository`, `importToFossil`, and `openFossilCheckout`.

**SUGGESTION 2: Component interfaces still reference `worktreePath`**

- **Location:** `components/ProjectDetailPage.tsx:19`, `components/SessionDetailPage.tsx:13`
- **Issue:** Session interface was updated but some component interfaces still have `worktreePath`. This was partially fixed but the interface shows both `upstreamPath` and `checkoutPath` - verify the Session type in these files matches the repository type.
- **Recommendation:** Verify `Session` interface in both component files matches the `Session` type from `sessions/repository.ts`.

**SUGGESTION 3: Missing return statement in agent sessions API**

- **Location:** `agents/routes.tsx:14-46`
- **Issue:** The `GET /me/sessions` route is placed before `router.use("/*", authMiddleware)` which means it won't have auth middleware applied. The route handles its own authentication, which is correct, but verify it returns early.
- **Recommendation:** Verify the response returns properly - the code looks correct but double-check the route ordering works as expected.

---

##### Spec Coverage Summary

<type>file</type>
<content>1: export interface VCSResult {
2:   success: boolean;
3:   output?: string;
4:   error?: string;
5:   port?: number;
6: }
7: 
8: export class VCS {
9:   private async execCommand(
10:     command: string[],
11:     cwd?: string
12:   ): Promise<{ success: boolean; output: string; error: string }> {
13:     const proc = Bun.spawn(command, {
14:       cwd,
15:       stdout: "pipe",
16:       stderr: "pipe",
17:     });
18: 
19:     const exitCode = await proc.exited;
20:     const stdout = await new Response(proc.stdout).text();
21:     const stderr = await new Response(proc.stderr).text();
22: 
23:     return {
24:       success: exitCode === 0,
25:       output: stdout.trim(),
26:       error: stderr.trim(),
27:     };
28:   }
29: 
30:   async checkFossilAvailable(): Promise<boolean> {
31:     const result = await this.execCommand(["fossil", "version"]);
32:     return result.success;
33:   }
34: 
35:   async getFossilVersion(): Promise<string | null> {
36:     const result = await this.execCommand(["fossil", "version"]);
37:     if (result.success) {
38:       const match = result.output.match(/(\d+\.\d+)/);
39:       return match ? match[1] : null;
40:     }
41:     return null;
42:   }
43: 
44:   async createFossilRepo(repoPath: string): Promise<VCSResult> {
45:     const result = await this.execCommand(["fossil", "init", repoPath]);
46:     return {
47:       success: result.success,
48:       output: result.output,
49:       error: result.error || undefined,
50:     };
51:   }
52: 
53:   async openFossil(repoPath: string, workDir: string): Promise<VCSResult> {
54:     const result = await this.execCommand(
55:       ["fossil", "open", repoPath],
56:       workDir
57:     );
58:     return {
59:       success: result.success,
60:       output: result.output,
61:       error: result.error || undefined,
62:     };
63:   }
64: 
65:   async importGitToFossil(gitUrl: string, workDir: string): Promise<VCSResult> {
66:     try {
67:       new URL(gitUrl);
68:     } catch {
69:       return {
70:         success: false,
71:         error: "Invalid Git URL format",
72:       };
73:     }
74: 
75:     // Create fossil repo first
76:     const fossilPath = `${workDir}/.fossil`;
77:     const initResult = await this.createFossilRepo(fossilPath);
78:     if (!initResult.success) {
79:       return initResult;
80:     }
81: 
82:     // Import from git
83:     const result = await this.execCommand(
84:       ["fossil", "import", "--git", gitUrl, fossilPath],
85:       workDir
86:     );
87: 
88:     if (result.success) {
89:       // Open the fossil repo in the workdir
90:       const openResult = await this.openFossil(fossilPath, workDir);
91:       return openResult;
92:     }
93: 
94:     return {
95:       success: false,
96:       output: result.output,
97:       error: result.error || "Failed to import from Git",
98:     };
99:   }
100: 
101:   async cloneFossil(
102:     sourcePath: string,
103:     targetDir: string
104:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
105:     const { mkdirSync } = await import("fs");
106:     const { dirname } = await import("path");
107: 
108:     // Ensure target directory exists
109:     try {
110:       mkdirSync(targetDir, { recursive: true });
111:     } catch {
112:       // Directory might already exist
113:     }
114: 
115:     // Clone the fossil repo
116:     const result = await this.execCommand([
117:       "fossil",
118:       "clone",
119:       sourcePath,
120:       `${targetDir}/.fossil`,
121:     ]);
122: 
123:     if (result.success) {
124:       // Open the cloned repo
125:       const openResult = await this.openFossil(
126:         `${targetDir}/.fossil`,
127:         targetDir
128:       );
129:       return openResult;
130:     }
131: 
132:     return {
133:       success: false,
134:       output: result.output,
135:       error: result.error || "Failed to clone Fossil repository",
136:     };
137:   }
138: 
139:   async sync(
140:     workDir: string,
141:     direction: "pull" | "push"
142:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
143:     const command = direction === "pull" ? "pull" : "push";
144:     const result = await this.execCommand(["fossil", command], workDir);
145: 
146:     return {
147:       success: result.success,
148:       output: result.output,
149:       error: result.error || undefined,
150:     };
151:   }
152: 
153:   async getStatus(workDir: string): Promise<VCSResult> {
154:     const result = await this.execCommand(["fossil", "changes"], workDir);
155:     return {
156:       success: result.success,
157:       output: result.output,
158:       error: result.error || undefined,
159:     };
160:   }
161: 
162:   async commit(workDir: string, message: string): Promise<VCSResult> {
163:     const result = await this.execCommand(
164:       ["fossil", "commit", "-m", message],
165:       workDir
166:     );
167: 
168:     return {
169:       success: result.success,
170:       output: result.output,
171:       error: result.error || undefined,
172:     };
173:   }
174: 
175:   async getCommitHistory(workDir: string, limit: number = 10): Promise<VCSResult> {
176:     const result = await this.execCommand(
177:       ["fossil", "timeline", "-n", limit.toString()],
178:       workDir
179:     );
180: 
181:     return {
182:       success: result.success,
183:       output: result.output,
184:       error: result.error || undefined,
185:     };
186:   }
187: 
188:   async setupSessionWorktree(
189:     projectId: string,
190:     sessionId: string,
191:     worktreePath: string
192:   ): Promise<VCSResult> {
193:     const { getProjectPath } = await import("../config/paths.js");
194:     const projectPath = getProjectPath(projectId);
195:     const fossilPath = `${projectPath}/repo.fossil`;
196: 
197:     // Ensure worktree directory exists
198:     const { mkdirSync } = await import("fs");
199:     try {
200:       mkdirSync(worktreePath, { recursive: true });
201:     } catch {
202:       // Directory might already exist
203:     }
204: 
205:     // Check if fossil repo exists
206:     const { existsSync } = await import("fs");
207:     if (!existsSync(fossilPath)) {
208:       return {
209:         success: false,
210:         error: "Project fossil repository not found",
211:       };
212:     }
213: 
214:     // Open the fossil repo in the worktree
215:     return await this.openFossil(fossilPath, worktreePath);

44:   private getSessionFilePath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
45:     return join(this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId), "session.yaml");
46:   }
47: 
48:   private generateId(): string {
49:     return crypto.randomUUID();
50:   }

52:   private getWorktreePath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
53:     return join(getPaths().projects, projectId, "worktrees", sessionId);
54:   }

56:   async create(input: CreateSessionInput): Promise<Session> {
57:     const id = this.generateId();
58:     const sessionPath = this.getSessionPath(input.projectId, id);
59:     const worktreePath = this.getWorktreePath(input.projectId, id);
60:     
61:     // Create session directory
62:     if (!existsSync(sessionPath)) {
63:       mkdirSync(sessionPath, { recursive: true });
64:     }
65: 
66:     // Create worktree directory
67:     if (!existsSync(worktreePath)) {
68:       mkdirSync(worktreePath, { recursive: true });
69:     }
70: 
71:     const now = new Date().toISOString();
72:     const sessionData: SessionData = {
73:       id,
74:       name: input.name,
75:       projectId: input.projectId,
76:       owner: input.owner,
77:       worktreePath,
78:       assignedAgentId: input.assignedAgentId,
79:       status: "active",
80:       createdAt: now,
81:       updatedAt: now,
82:     };
83: 
84:     writeFileSync(
85:       this.getSessionFilePath(input.projectId, id),
86:       dump(sessionData),
87:       "utf-8"
88:     );
89: 
90:     return {
91:       ...sessionData,
92:       createdAt: new Date(sessionData.createdAt),
93:       updatedAt: new Date(sessionData.updatedAt),
94:     };
95:   }
96: 
97:   async findById(sessionId: string): Promise<Session | null> {
98:     // Search across all projects for the session
99:     const Paths = getPaths();
100:     if (!existsSync(Paths.projects)) {
101:       return null;
102:     }
103: 
104:     const projectEntries = readdirSync(Paths.projects, { withFileTypes: true });
105:     
106:     for (const projectEntry of projectEntries) {
107:       if (projectEntry.isDirectory()) {
108:         const sessionsDir = join(Paths.projects, projectEntry.name, "sessions");
109:         if (existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
110:           const sessionFile = join(sessionsDir, sessionId, "session.yaml");
111:           if (existsSync(sessionFile)) {
112:             const content = readFileSync(sessionFile, "utf-8");
113:             const data = load(content) as SessionData;
114:             return {
115:               ...data,
116:               createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
117:               updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
118:             };
119:           }
120:         }
121:       }
122:     }
123: 
124:     return null;
125:   }
126: 
127:   async findByProjectAndId(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<Session | null> {
128:     const filePath = this.getSessionFilePath(projectId, sessionId);
129:     if (!existsSync(filePath)) {
130:       return null;
131:     }
132: 
133:     const content = readFileSync(filePath, "utf-8");
134:     const data = load(content) as SessionData;
135:     
136:     return {

143:   async listByProject(projectId: string): Promise<Session[]> {
144:     const sessionsDir = join(getPaths().projects, projectId, "sessions");
145:     if (!existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
146:       return [];
147:     }
148: 
149:     const entries = readdirSync(sessionsDir, { withFileTypes: true });
150:     const sessions: Session[] = [];
151: 
152:     for (const entry of entries) {
153:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
154:         const sessionFile = join(sessionsDir, entry.name, "session.yaml");
155:         if (existsSync(sessionFile)) {
156:           const content = readFileSync(sessionFile, "utf-8");
157:           const data = load(content) as SessionData;
158:           sessions.push({
159:             ...data,
160:             createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
161:             updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
162:           });
163:         }
164:       }
165:     }
166: 
167:     return sessions.sort((a, b) => b.createdAt.getTime() - a.createdAt.getTime());
168:   }
169: 
170:   async findByAssignedAgentId(agentId: string): Promise<Session[]> {
171:     const Paths = getPaths();
172:     if (!existsSync(Paths.projects)) {
173:       return [];
174:     }
175: 
176:     const projectEntries = readdirSync(Paths.projects, { withFileTypes: true });
177:     const sessions: Session[] = [];
178: 
179:     for (const projectEntry of projectEntries) {
180:       if (projectEntry.isDirectory()) {
181:         const sessionsDir = join(Paths.projects, projectEntry.name, "sessions");
182:         if (existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
183:           const entries = readdirSync(sessionsDir, { withFileTypes: true });
184:           for (const entry of entries) {
185:             if (entry.isDirectory()) {
186:               const sessionFile = join(sessionsDir, entry.name, "session.yaml");
187:               if (existsSync(sessionFile)) {
188:                 const content = readFileSync(sessionFile, "utf-8");
189:                 const data = load(content) as SessionData;
190:                 if (data.assignedAgentId === agentId) {
191:                   sessions.push({
192:                     ...data,
193:                     createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
194:                     updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
195:                   });
196:                 }
197:               }
198:             }
199:           }
200:         }
201:       }
202:     }
203: 
204:     return sessions.sort((a, b) => b.createdAt.getTime() - a.createdAt.getTime());
205:   }
206: 
207:   async update(sessionId: string, updates: Partial<Omit<SessionData, "id" | "createdAt">>): Promise<Session | null> {
208:     const session = await this.findById(sessionId);
209:     if (!session) return null;
210: 
211:     const updatedData: SessionData = {
212:       ...session,
213:       ...updates,
214:       updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
215:     };
216: 
217:     const filePath = this.getSessionFilePath(session.projectId, sessionId);
218:     writeFileSync(filePath, dump(updatedData), "utf-8");
219: 
220:     return {
221:       ...updatedData,
222:       createdAt: new Date(updatedData.createdAt),
223:       updatedAt: new Date(updatedData.updatedAt),
224:     };
225:   }
226: 
227:   async delete(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
228:     const sessionPath = this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId);
229:     
230:     // Get session to find worktree path
231:     const session = await this.findByProjectAndId(projectId, sessionId);
232:     
233:     if (session && existsSync(session.worktreePath)) {
234:       // Delete worktree directory
235:       this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(session.worktreePath);
236:     }
237:     
238:     // Delete session directory
239:     if (existsSync(sessionPath)) {
240:       this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(sessionPath);
241:     }
242:   }
243: 
244:   private deleteDirectoryRecursive(dirPath: string): void {
245:     if (!existsSync(dirPath)) return;
246: 
247:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
248:     
249:     for (const entry of entries) {
250:       const entryPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
251:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
252:         this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(entryPath);
253:       } else {
254:         unlinkSync(entryPath);
255:       }
256:     }
257: 
258:     rmdirSync(dirPath);
259:   }
260: 
261:   async exists(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<boolean> {
262:     return existsSync(this.getSessionFilePath(projectId, sessionId));
263:   }
264: }

31: interface FileChange {
32:   path: string;
33:   status: "clean" | "modified" | "new" | "deleted" | "conflict";
34: }
35: 
36: interface SessionDetailProps {
37:   project: Project;
38:   session: Session;
39:   chatHistory: ChatMessage[];
40:   agent?: Agent;
41:   changes?: FileChange[];
42:   hasConflicts?: boolean;
43: }
44: 
45: function renderFileTree(changes: FileChange[]) {
46:   const fileTree: Map<string, { name: string; status: FileChange["status"] }[]> = new Map();
47:   
48:   for (const change of changes) {
49:     const parts = change.path.split("/");
50:     const fileName = parts.pop() || "";
51:     const dir = parts.length > 0 ? parts.join("/") : "(root)";
52:     
53:     if (!fileTree.has(dir)) {
54:       fileTree.set(dir, []);
55:     }
56:     fileTree.get(dir)!.push({ name: fileName, status: change.status });
57:   }
58:   
59:   const sortedDirs = Array.from(fileTree.entries()).sort((a, b) => a[0].localeCompare(b[0]));
60:   
61:   return (
62:     <div class="file-tree">
63:       {sortedDirs.map(([dir, files]) => (
64:         <div key={dir} class="file-tree-dir">
65:           <div class="file-tree-dir-name">{dir}/</div>
66:           <div class="file-tree-files">
67:             {files.map((file) => (
68:               <div key={file.name} class="file-tree-file">
69:                 <span class={`file-indicator file-indicator-${file.status}`}>
70:                   {file.status === "modified" && "[M]"}
71:                   {file.status === "new" && "[?]"}
72:                   {file.status === "deleted" && "[D]"}
73:                   {file.status === "conflict" && "[!]"}
74:                   {file.status === "clean" && "   "}
75:                 </span>
76:                 <span class={`file-name file-name-${file.status}`}>{file.name}</span>
77:               </div>
78:             ))}
79:           </div>
80:         </div>
81:       ))}
82:     </div>
83:   );
84: }
85: 
86: function getStatusIcon(status: FileChange["status"]): string {
87:   switch (status) {
88:     case "modified": return "M";
89:     case "new": return "?";
90:     case "deleted": return "D";
91:     case "conflict": return "!";
92:     default: return " ";
93:   }
94: }
95:

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 01:23:42)

The error is happening during the `importToFossil` step. The issue is that `fossil import --git` expects a path to a git bundle or a git repository, but we're passing the `.git` directory path incorrectly.

Looking at the error:
```
open(/home/bit4bit/.mimo/projects/7387445d-33c2-4f1e-b6cd-6f3539ab4979/sessions/21010368-d59e-4491-96b6-0b6877e401ec/upstream/.git) - Is a directory
```

The issue is in `vcs/index.ts` in the `importToFossil` function. The `fossil import --git` command expects either:
1. A git bundle file
2. A git fast-export stream on stdin

Not a `.git` directory path directly.

Let me check the correct way to do this. The `fossil import --git` command reads from stdin or from a file. We need to pipe the output of `git fast-export` to `fossil import --git`.

Actually, looking at fossil documentation, the correct approach is:
```
git fast-export --all | fossil import --git repo.fossil
```

Or we can use `--git` flag with a git repository path, but that needs the repository root, not the `.git` directory.

Let me fix the `importToFossil` function.

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 01:23:49)

The issue is that `fossil import --git` doesn't work the way I implemented it. Looking at fossil documentation:

1. `fossil import --git REPOFOSSIL` reads git fast-export format from stdin
2. We need to pipe `git fast-export` output into `fossil import --git REPOFOSSIL`

The correct approach is:
1. Create fossil repo first
2. Run `git fast-export --all` in the upstream directory, pipe to `fossil import --git fossilPath`

Let me fix this.
## Agent (2026-04-04 01:23:51)

The issue is that `fossil import --git` expects git fast-export format on stdin, not a `.git` directory path. We need to pipe `git fast-export` to `fossil import`.

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/vcs/index.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:24:00
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/vcs/index.ts
newString:   async importToFossil(
    upstreamPath: string,
    repoType: "git" | "fossil",
    fossilPath: string
  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
    if (repoType === "git") {
      // Import from Git to Fossil using git fast-export
      // First create the fossil repo
      const initResult = await this.createFossilRepo(fossilPath);
      if (!initResult.success) {
        return initResult;
      }
      
      // Use git fast-export piped to fossil import
      // We need to run: git fast-export --all | fossil import --git fossilPath
      const result = await new Promise<{ success: boolean; output: string; error: string }>((resolve) => {
        const { spawn } = require("child_process");
        
        const gitExport = spawn("git", ["fast-export", "--all"], { cwd: upstreamPath });
        const fossilImport = spawn("fossil", ["import", "--git", fossilPath], { cwd: upstreamPath });
        
        let stdout = "";
        let stderr = "";
        
        gitExport.stdout.pipe(fossilImport.stdin);
        
        fossilImport.stdout.on("data", (data) => {
          stdout += data.toString();
        });
        
        fossilImport.stderr.on("data", (data) => {
          stderr += data.toString();
        });
        
        gitExport.stderr.on("data", (data) => {
          stderr += data.toString();
        });
        
        fossilImport.on("close", (code) => {
          resolve({
            success: code === 0,
            output: stdout,
            error: stderr,
          });
        });
        
        gitExport.on("error", (err) => {
          fossilImport.kill();
          resolve({
            success: false,
            output: "",
            error: `Git fast-export failed: ${err.message}`,
          });
        });
      });
      
      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    } else {
      // For fossil, clone from the upstream fossil repo
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["fossil", "clone", `${upstreamPath}/.fossil`, fossilPath],
        upstreamPath
      );
      
      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    }
  }
oldString:   async importToFossil(
    upstreamPath: string,
    repoType: "git" | "fossil",
    fossilPath: string
  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
    if (repoType === "git") {
      // Import from Git to Fossil
      // First create the fossil repo
      const initResult = await this.createFossilRepo(fossilPath);
      if (!initResult.success) {
        return initResult;
      }
      
      // Import from git bundle or directory
      const gitDir = `${upstreamPath}/.git`;
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["fossil", "import", "--git", gitDir, fossilPath],
        upstreamPath
      );
      
      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    } else {
      // For fossil, clone from the upstream fossil repo
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["fossil", "clone", `${upstreamPath}/.fossil`, fossilPath],
        upstreamPath
      );
      
      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    }
  }

```

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 01:24:51)

The error shows that the table "blob" already exists. This means we're trying to create a new fossil repo that already exists, or we're importing into a fossil repo that was already created.

Looking at the flow:
1. We create the fossil repo with `createFossilRepo(fossilPath)`
2. Then we try to import with `fossil import --git`

But wait - the issue is that `fossil import --git` creates its own repository if one doesn't exist, OR it might be that we're calling `createFossilRepo` first and THEN trying to import, which causes issues because fossil import also creates the repo.

Let me check the fossil documentation - `fossil import --git` should be able to create the repo automatically when given a filename that doesn't exist.

Actually, I think the issue is:
1. We call `createFossilRepo(fossilPath)` which creates an empty fossil database
2. Then we call `fossil import --git` which ALSO tries to create the database structure

The fix should be to NOT create the fossil repo separately - just let `fossil import --git` create it.
## Agent (2026-04-04 01:24:53)

The issue is that we're creating an empty fossil repo first with `createFossilRepo`, then `fossil import --git` tries to create tables that already exist. The `fossil import` command creates the repository itself - we don't need to initialize it separately.

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/vcs/index.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:25:06
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/vcs/index.ts
newString:   async importToFossil(
    upstreamPath: string,
    repoType: "git" | "fossil",
    fossilPath: string
  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
    if (repoType === "git") {
      // Import from Git to Fossil using git fast-export
      // fossil import --git creates the repo automatically
      
      // Use git fast-export piped to fossil import
      // We need to run: git fast-export --all | fossil import --git fossilPath
      const result = await new Promise<{ success: boolean; output: string; error: string }>((resolve) => {
        const { spawn } = require("child_process");
        
        const gitExport = spawn("git", ["fast-export", "--all"], { cwd: upstreamPath });
        const fossilImport = spawn("fossil", ["import", "--git", fossilPath], { cwd: upstreamPath });
        
        let stdout = "";
        let stderr = "";
        
        gitExport.stdout.pipe(fossilImport.stdin);
        
        fossilImport.stdout.on("data", (data) => {
          stdout += data.toString();
        });
        
        fossilImport.stderr.on("data", (data) => {
          stderr += data.toString();
        });
        
        gitExport.stderr.on("data", (data) => {
          stderr += data.toString();
        });
        
        fossilImport.on("close", (code) => {
          resolve({
            success: code === 0,
            output: stdout,
            error: stderr,
          });
        });
        
        gitExport.on("error", (err) => {
          fossilImport.kill();
          resolve({
            success: false,
            output: "",
            error: `Git fast-export failed: ${err.message}`,
          });
        });
      });
      
      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    } else {
      // For fossil, clone from the upstream fossil repo
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["fossil", "clone", `${upstreamPath}/.fossil`, fossilPath],
        upstreamPath
      );
      
      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    }
  }
oldString:   async importToFossil(
    upstreamPath: string,
    repoType: "git" | "fossil",
    fossilPath: string
  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
    if (repoType === "git") {
      // Import from Git to Fossil using git fast-export
      // First create the fossil repo
      const initResult = await this.createFossilRepo(fossilPath);
      if (!initResult.success) {
        return initResult;
      }
      
      // Use git fast-export piped to fossil import
      // We need to run: git fast-export --all | fossil import --git fossilPath
      const result = await new Promise<{ success: boolean; output: string; error: string }>((resolve) => {
        const { spawn } = require("child_process");
        
        const gitExport = spawn("git", ["fast-export", "--all"], { cwd: upstreamPath });
        const fossilImport = spawn("fossil", ["import", "--git", fossilPath], { cwd: upstreamPath });
        
        let stdout = "";
        let stderr = "";
        
        gitExport.stdout.pipe(fossilImport.stdin);
        
        fossilImport.stdout.on("data", (data) => {
          stdout += data.toString();
        });
        
        fossilImport.stderr.on("data", (data) => {
          stderr += data.toString();
        });
        
        gitExport.stderr.on("data", (data) => {
          stderr += data.toString();
        });
        
        fossilImport.on("close", (code) => {
          resolve({
            success: code === 0,
            output: stdout,
            error: stderr,
          });
        });
        
        gitExport.on("error", (err) => {
          fossilImport.kill();
          resolve({
            success: false,
            output: "",
            error: `Git fast-export failed: ${err.message}`,
          });
        });
      });
      
      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    } else {
      // For fossil, clone from the upstream fossil repo
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["fossil", "clone", `${upstreamPath}/.fossil`, fossilPath],
        upstreamPath
      );
      
      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    }
  }

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/test/session-bootstrap.test.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:26:05
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/test/session-bootstrap.test.ts
content: import { describe, it, expect, beforeEach, afterEach } from "bun:test";
import { tmpdir } from "os";
import { join } from "path";
import { rmSync, existsSync, mkdirSync, writeFileSync } from "fs";
import { execSync } from "child_process";

describe("Session Bootstrap Integration Tests", () => {
  let testHome: string;
  let VCS: any;
  let SessionRepository: any;
  let sessionRepository: any;

  beforeEach(async () => {
    testHome = join(tmpdir(), `mimo-bootstrap-test-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8)}`);
    process.env.MIMO_HOME = testHome;
    
    // Clean up from previous run
    try {
      rmSync(testHome, { recursive: true, force: true });
    } catch {}
    
    mkdirSync(testHome, { recursive: true });
    mkdirSync(join(testHome, "projects"), { recursive: true });

    // Re-import to get fresh modules
    const vcsModule = await import("../src/vcs/index.ts");
    VCS = vcsModule.VCS;

    const sessionModule = await import("../src/sessions/repository.ts");
    SessionRepository = sessionModule.SessionRepository;
    sessionRepository = sessionModule.sessionRepository;
  });

  afterEach(() => {
    try {
      rmSync(testHome, { recursive: true, force: true });
    } catch {}
  });

  describe("Git Repository Bootstrap", () => {
    it("should clone a Git repository to upstream directory", async () => {
      const vcs = new VCS();
      const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "test-upstream");
      
      // Clone a small public repo
      const result = await vcs.cloneRepository(
        "https://github.com/octocat/Hello-World.git",
        "git",
        upstreamPath
      );

      expect(result.success).toBe(true);
      expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git"))).toBe(true);
    }, 30000);

    it("should import Git repository to Fossil", async () => {
      const vcs = new VCS();
      const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "import-test");
      const fossilPath = join(testHome, "import-test.fossil");
      
      // Create a simple git repo
      mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
      execSync("git init", { cwd: upstreamPath });
      writeFileSync(join(upstreamPath, "README.md"), "# Test");
      execSync("git add .", { cwd: upstreamPath });
      execSync('git commit -m "Initial commit"', { cwd: upstreamPath });
      
      // Import to fossil
      const result = await vcs.importToFossil(upstreamPath, "git", fossilPath);
      
      expect(result.success).toBe(true);
      expect(existsSync(fossilPath)).toBe(true);
    }, 15000);

    it("should open Fossil checkout", async () => {
      const vcs = new VCS();
      const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "checkout-test");
      const fossilPath = join(testHome, "checkout-test.fossil");
      const checkoutPath = join(testHome, "checkout");
      
      // Create a simple git repo
      mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
      execSync("git init", { cwd: upstreamPath });
      writeFileSync(join(upstreamPath, "README.md"), "# Test");
      execSync("git add .", { cwd: upstreamPath });
      execSync('git commit -m "Initial commit"', { cwd: upstreamPath });
      
      // Import to fossil
      await vcs.importToFossil(upstreamPath, "git", fossilPath);
      
      // Open checkout
      const result = await vcs.openFossilCheckout(fossilPath, checkoutPath);
      
      expect(result.success).toBe(true);
      expect(existsSync(join(checkoutPath, "README.md"))).toBe(true);
    }, 15000);

    it("should fail on invalid Git URL", async () => {
      const vcs = new VCS();
      const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "invalid-url");
      
      const result = await vcs.cloneRepository(
        "not-a-url",
        "git",
        upstreamPath
      );

      expect(result.success).toBe(false);
      expect(result.error).toBeDefined();
    }, 10000);
  });

  describe("Fossil Repository Bootstrap", () => {
    it("should clone a Fossil repository", async () => {
      const vcs = new VCS();
      
      // First create a fossil repo to clone from
      const sourcePath = join(testHome, "source.fossil");
      await vcs.createFossilRepo(sourcePath);
      
      const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "fossil-upstream");
      const result = await vcs.cloneFossil(sourcePath, upstreamPath);
      
      expect(result.success).toBe(true);
      expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, ".fossil"))).toBe(true);
    }, 15000);
  });

  describe("Session Repository", () => {
    it("should create session with upstream and checkout directories", async () => {
      const session = await sessionRepository.create({
        name: "Test Session",
        projectId: "test-project-id",
        owner: "testuser",
      });

      expect(session).toBeDefined();
      expect(session.id).toBeDefined();
      expect(session.upstreamPath).toBeDefined();
      expect(session.checkoutPath).toBeDefined();
      
      // Verify directories were created
      expect(existsSync(session.upstreamPath)).toBe(true);
      expect(existsSync(session.checkoutPath)).toBe(true);
    });

    it("should store upstreamPath and checkoutPath in session.yaml", async () => {
      const session = await sessionRepository.create({
        name: "Path Test",
        projectId: "test-project",
        owner: "testuser",
      });

      // Load the session again
      const loaded = await sessionRepository.findById(session.id);
      
      expect(loaded).not.toBeNull();
      expect(loaded?.upstreamPath).toBe(session.upstreamPath);
      expect(loaded?.checkoutPath).toBe(session.checkoutPath);
    });

    it("should delete session directory including upstream and checkout", async () => {
      const session = await sessionRepository.create({
        name: "Delete Test",
        projectId: "test-project",
        owner: "testuser",
      });

      // Verify paths exist
      expect(existsSync(session.upstreamPath)).toBe(true);
      expect(existsSync(session.checkoutPath)).toBe(true);

      // Delete
      await sessionRepository.delete("test-project", session.id);

      // Verify deleted
      const loaded = await sessionRepository.findById(session.id);
      expect(loaded).toBeNull();
    });
  });

  describe("Full Bootstrap Flow", () => {
    it("should bootstrap a session from Git repository", async () => {
      const vcs = new VCS();
      const projectId = "full-bootstrap-test";
      const projectPath = join(testHome, "projects", projectId);
      mkdirSync(projectPath, { recursive: true });

      // Create session
      const session = await sessionRepository.create({
        name: "Full Bootstrap",
        projectId,
        owner: "testuser",
      });

      // Clone upstream
      const cloneResult = await vcs.cloneRepository(
        "https://github.com/octocat/Hello-World.git",
        "git",
        session.upstreamPath
      );
      expect(cloneResult.success).toBe(true);

      // Import to fossil
      const fossilPath = join(session.upstreamPath, "..", "repo.fossil");
      const importResult = await vcs.importToFossil(
        session.upstreamPath,
        "git",
        fossilPath
      );
      expect(importResult.success).toBe(true);

      // Open checkout
      const checkoutResult = await vcs.openFossilCheckout(
        fossilPath,
        session.checkoutPath
      );
      expect(checkoutResult.success).toBe(true);

      // Verify files exist in checkout
      expect(existsSync(join(session.checkoutPath, "README"))).toBe(true);
    }, 60000);
  });
});

+import { describe, it, expect, beforeEach, afterEach } from "bun:test";
+import { tmpdir } from "os";
+import { join } from "path";
+import { rmSync, existsSync, mkdirSync, writeFileSync } from "fs";
+import { execSync } from "child_process";
+
+describe("Session Bootstrap Integration Tests", () => {
+  let testHome: string;
+  let VCS: any;
+  let SessionRepository: any;
+  let sessionRepository: any;
+
+  beforeEach(async () => {
+    testHome = join(tmpdir(), `mimo-bootstrap-test-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8)}`);
+    process.env.MIMO_HOME = testHome;
+    
+    // Clean up from previous run
+    try {
+      rmSync(testHome, { recursive: true, force: true });
+    } catch {}
+    
+    mkdirSync(testHome, { recursive: true });
+    mkdirSync(join(testHome, "projects"), { recursive: true });
+
+    // Re-import to get fresh modules
+    const vcsModule = await import("../src/vcs/index.ts");
+    VCS = vcsModule.VCS;
+
+    const sessionModule = await import("../src/sessions/repository.ts");
+    SessionRepository = sessionModule.SessionRepository;
+    sessionRepository = sessionModule.sessionRepository;
+  });
+
+  afterEach(() => {
+    try {
+      rmSync(testHome, { recursive: true, force: true });
+    } catch {}
+  });
+
+  describe("Git Repository Bootstrap", () => {
+    it("should clone a Git repository to upstream directory", async () => {
+      const vcs = new VCS();
+      const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "test-upstream");
+      
+      // Clone a small public repo
+      const result = await vcs.cloneRepository(
+        "https://github.com/octocat/Hello-World.git",
+        "git",
+        upstreamPath
+      );
+
+      expect(result.success).toBe(true);
+      expect(existsSync(join(upstreamPath, ".git"))).toBe(true);
+    }, 30000);
+
+    it("should import Git repository to Fossil", async () => {
+      const vcs = new VCS();
+      const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "import-test");
+      const fossilPath = join(testHome, "import-test.fossil");
+      
+      // Create a simple git repo
+      mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
+      execSync("git init", { cwd: upstreamPath });
+      writeFileSync(join(upstreamPath, "README.md"), "# Test");
+      execSync("git add .", { cwd: upstreamPath });
+      execSync('git commit -m "Initial commit"', { cwd: upstreamPath });
+      
+      // Import to fossil
+      const result = await vcs.importToFossil(upstreamPath, "git", fossilPath);
+      
+      expect(result.success).toBe(true);
+      expect(existsSync(fossilPath)).toBe(true);
+    }, 15000);
+
+    it("should open Fossil checkout", async () => {
+      const vcs = new VCS();
+      const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "checkout-test");
+      const fossilPath = join(testHome, "checkout-test.fossil");
+      const checkoutPath = join(testHome, "checkout");
+      
+      // Create a simple git repo
+      mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
+      execSync("git init", { cwd: upstreamPath });
+      writeFileSync(join(upstreamPath, "README.md"), "# Test");
+      execSync("git add .", { cwd: upstreamPath });
+      execSync('git commit -m "Initial commit"', { cwd: upstreamPath });
+      
+      // Import to fossil
+      await vcs.importToFossil(upstreamPath, "git", fossilPath);
+      
+      // Open checkout
+      const result = await vcs.openFossilCheckout(fossilPath, checkoutPath);
+      
+      expect(result.success).toBe(true);
+      expect(existsSync(join(checkoutPath, "README.md"))).toBe(true);
+    }, 15000);
+
+    it("should fail on invalid Git URL", async () => {
+      const vcs = new VCS();
+      const upstreamPath = join(testHome, "invalid-url");
+      
+      const result = await vcs.cloneRepository(
+        "not-a-url",

+        upstreamPath

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/test/fossil-server.test.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 01:26:22
**Parameters:**
content: import { describe, it, expect, beforeEach, afterEach } from "bun:test";
import { tmpdir } from "os";
import { join } from "path";
import { rmSync, existsSync, mkdirSync } from "fs";

describe("Fossil Server Manager Integration Tests", () => {
  let testHome: string;
  let FossilServerManager: any;
  let fossilServerManager: any;
  let VCS: any;

  beforeEach(async () => {
    testHome = join(tmpdir(), `mimo-fossil-server-test-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8)}`);
    process.env.MIMO_HOME = testHome;
    
    // Clean up from previous run
    try {
      rmSync(testHome, { recursive: true, force: true });
    } catch {}
    
    mkdirSync(testHome, { recursive: true });

    // Re-import to get fresh modules
    const vcsModule = await import("../src/vcs/index.ts");
    VCS = vcsModule.VCS;

    const serverModule = await import("../src/vcs/fossil-server.ts");
    FossilServerManager = serverModule.FossilServerManager;
    fossilServerManager = serverModule.fossilServerManager;
  });

  afterEach(async () => {
    // Stop all servers
    try {
      await fossilServerManager.stopAllServers();
    } catch {}
    
    try {
      rmSync(testHome, { recursive: true, force: true });
    } catch {}
  });

  describe("Port Management", () => {
    it("should assign ports in 8000-9000 range", () => {
      const port = fossilServerManager.assignPort();
      
      expect(port).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(8000);
      expect(port).toBeLessThanOrEqual(9000);
    });

    it("should assign unique ports", () => {
      const port1 = fossilServerManager.assignPort();
      const port2 = fossilServerManager.assignPort();
      
      expect(port1).not.toBe(port2);
    });

    it("should release ports", () => {
      const port = fossilServerManager.assignPort();
      fossilServerManager.releasePort(port);
      
      // Port should be available again
      const newPort = fossilServerManager.assignPort();
      // Not guaranteed to be the same, but should be in range
      expect(newPort).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(8000);
      expect(newPort).toBeLessThanOrEqual(9000);
    });
  });

  describe("Server Lifecycle", () => {
    it("should start a Fossil server", async () => {
      const vcs = new VCS();
      const repoPath = join(testHome, "test.fossil");
      await vcs.createFossilRepo(repoPath);

      const result = await fossilServerManager.startServer("test-session", repoPath);

      expect(result.port).toBeDefined();
      expect(result.port).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(8000);
      expect(result.port).toBeLessThanOrEqual(9000);

      // Server should be tracked
      expect(fossilServerManager.isServerRunning("test-session")).toBe(true);

      // Cleanup
      await fossilServerManager.stopServer("test-session");
    }, 15000);

    it("should stop a Fossil server", async () => {
      const vcs = new VCS();
      const repoPath = join(testHome, "stop-test.fossil");
      await vcs.createFossilRepo(repoPath);

      await fossilServerManager.startServer("stop-session", repoPath);
      expect(fossilServerManager.isServerRunning("stop-session")).toBe(true);

      await fossilServerManager.stopServer("stop-session");
      expect(fossilServerManager.isServerRunning("stop-session")).toBe(false);
    }, 15000);

    it("should return existing server for same session", async () => {
      const vcs = new VCS();
      const repoPath = join(testHome, "existing.fossil");
      await vcs.createFossilRepo(repoPath);

      const result1 = await fossilServerManager.startServer("existing-session", repoPath);
      const result2 = await fossilServerManager.startServer("existing-session", repoPath);

      expect(result1.port).toBe(result2.port);

      // Cleanup
      await fossilServerManager.stopServer("existing-session");
    }, 15000);

    it("should fail with PORTS_EXHAUSTED when no ports available", async () => {
      const vcs = new VCS();
      const repoPath = join(testHome, "exhausted.fossil");
      await vcs.createFossilRepo(repoPath);

      // Exhaust all ports
      const ports: number[] = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < 1001; i++) {
        const port = fossilServerManager.assignPort();
        ports.push(port);
      }

      // Try to start server - should fail
      const result = await fossilServerManager.startServer("exhausted-session", repoPath);
      expect(result.error).toBe("PORTS_EXHAUSTED");

      // Release ports
      ports.forEach(port => fossilServerManager.releasePort(port));
    }, 20000);

    it("should fail if repo file does not exist", async () => {
      const result = await fossilServerManager.startServer(
        "nonexistent-session",
        "/nonexistent/path.fossil"
      );

      expect(result.error).toContain("Repository not found");
    });
  });

  describe("Server Tracking", () => {
    it("should track running servers", async () => {
      const vcs = new VCS();
      const repoPath1 = join(testHome, "track1.fossil");
      const repoPath2 = join(testHome, "track2.fossil");
      await vcs.createFossilRepo(repoPath1);
      await vcs.createFossilRepo(repoPath2);

      await fossilServerManager.startServer("session-1", repoPath1);
      await fossilServerManager.startServer("session-2", repoPath2);

      expect(fossilServerManager.getActiveServerCount()).toBe(2);
      expect(fossilServerManager.isServerRunning("session-1")).toBe(true);
      expect(fossilServerManager.isServerRunning("session-2")).toBe(true);

      await fossilServerManager.stopAllServers();
      expect(fossilServerManager.getActiveServerCount()).toBe(0);
    }, 15000);

    it("should return server info for running server", async () => {
      const vcs = new VCS();
      const repoPath = join(testHome, "info.fossil");
      await vcs.createFossilRepo(repoPath);

      const result = await fossilServerManager.startServer("info-session", repoPath);
      const info = fossilServerManager.getRunningServer("info-session");

      expect(info).not.toBeNull();
      expect(info?.port).toBe(result.port);
      expect(info?.repoPath).toBe(repoPath);

      await fossilServerManager.stopServer("info-session");
    }, 15000);

    it("should return null for non-running server", () => {
      const info = fossilServerManager.getRunningServer("nonexistent");
      expect(info).toBeNull();
    });
  });
});
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/test/fossil-server.test.ts

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 01:26:25)

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/test/agent-sessions.test.ts

**Tool:** edit
